# 2.3 PsCell

## 2.3.1 General

**2.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `10966440`)

General
Description: Control of NRCELLGRPs (Cell Groups) and cells.

Used by: 5G-CP-RT

Addressing: [5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_58\_replaced([11176868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeQodvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

---

## 2.3.2 Procedures

### 2.3.2.0-1 Procedures Document Owner N/A (ID: 10966451)

### 2.3.2.1 Cell Group Setup

#### 2.3.2.1.0-3 Cell Group Setup Overview (ID: 10966469)

**2.3.2.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12729149`)

Cell Group Setup
Messages:

PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq/Resp

Purpose:

To setup the common parameters for cells of a NRCELLGRP (see 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Address distribution in PsCnfg interface is done.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_76\_replaced([11177702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeU55fvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell setup and L1 subcells setup.

---

#### 2.3.2.1.0-4 Cell Group Setup Description (ID: 10966475)

**2.3.2.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12730315`)

Cell Group Setup
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update the cell group context for the common parameters share in one NRCELLGRP, which are provided in the message and all related cell resources.

The new values shall be valid for all UEs in the cells.

**[5GC000998-A] Link is done between DL /UL scheduler couple and a new value of nrcellgrpid. It triggers sending of message LoCtrl\_AddressReq to 5G-L2-LO. See [5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_80\_replaced([11177738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeU56vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].**

NOTE: the nrCellList is updated internally by L2-PS at Cell addition (See 5G\_L2\_IF\_53\_replaced([10966872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQ3PPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) step.

---

#### 2.3.2.1.0-5 Cell Group Setup Message validation (ID: 10966480)

**2.3.2.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12730318`)

Cell Group Setup
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupSetupResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the cell group was setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_5928\_replaced([10966492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCBPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.1.0-6 Cell Group Setup Concurrency handling (ID: 10966486)

**2.3.2.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12730358`)

Cell Group Setup
Concurrent Cell Group procedures are not managed at L2-RT side.

If a Cell Group Setup procedure is initiated by 5G-CP-RT, no other Cell Group procedures (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated, until the on-going Cell Group Setup procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.1.0-7 Cell Group Setup Exceptions (ID: 10966492)

**2.3.2.1.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `13405939`)

Cell Group Setup
**Expected Exceptions:**

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* nrCellGrpId IE is not valid or it already exists or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not allocated successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that rollback is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS.

In PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq message , if IE actDpaOverloadControl = true, but then actK1Opt is disabled in PsCell\_CellSetupReq in 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then the actDpaOverloadControl can't trigger the real DPA overload control as 5G\_L2\_15833\_replaced([11158816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25Mm7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G-L2-PS should give a WRN log.

If actDpaOverloadControl can trigger the real DPA overload control, but IE actAdaptiveSchedulerBudgetOlc = false in PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq message, then the general adptive overload control is not enabled as expected, so no interworking between DPA overload control and general oveload control shoule be done. 5G-L2-PS should give a WRN log.

In PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq message , if IE actDpaOverloadControl = true, and the L2PS is not on Snowfish or Marlin [CB014419-SR-EC] or Nemo [End CB014419-SR-EC], actDpaOverloadControl can't trigger the real DPA overload control as 5G\_L2\_15833\_replaced([11158816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25Mm7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), set actDpaOverloadControl = false in L2PS as if actDpaOverloadControl = false in the PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq message.

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

### 2.3.2.2 Cell Group Delete

#### 2.3.2.2.0-2 Cell Group Delete Overview (ID: 10966653)

**2.3.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12732207`)

Cell Group Delete
Messages:

PsCell\_CellGroupDeleteReq/Resp

Purpose:

Cell Group and all cells (and subcells) belonging to a NRCELLGRP (see 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be deleted by 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Cell group exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_91\_replaced([11178210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeXWL_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell delete

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-3 Cell Group Delete Description (ID: 10966659)

**2.3.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12732209`)

Cell Group Delete
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall delete the cell group context and all related cell resources (including all the subcells).

5G-L2-PS shall also remove the related NRCELL objects from PM, see 5G\_L2\_1517\_replaced([11192164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOzPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[Before 5GC000559-C]**

If the cell group context does not exist, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the procedure is successful and return a response accordingly.

**[End 5GC000559-C]**

NOTE: the nrCellList is updated internally by L2-PS at  Cell deletion (See 5G\_L2\_IF\_182\_replaced([10970526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjLH_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) step.

**[5GC000998-L]**

DL/UL scheduler couple allocated to this NrCellGrpId shall be freed.

**[End 5GC000998-L]**

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-4 Cell Group Delete Message validation (ID: 10966666)

**2.3.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12732210`)

Cell Group Delete
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellGroupDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupDeleteResp message if the request message is valid, the cell group identified and deleted successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_37\_replaced([10966677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPpH_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-5 Cell Group Delete Concurrency handling (ID: 10966671)

**2.3.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12732212`)

Cell Group Delete
Concurrent Cell Group procedures are not managed at L2-RT side.

If a Cell Group Delete procedure is initiated by 5G-CP-RT, no other Cell Group procedures (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated , until the on-going Cell Group Delete procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-6 Cell Group Delete Exceptions (ID: 10966677)

**2.3.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12732214`)

Cell Group Delete
Expected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-C]

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupDeleteResp message also if:

* nrCellGrpId IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not deleted successfully.

[End 5GC000559-C]

Unexpected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-C]

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

[End 5GC000559-C]

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-7 Cell Group Delete PsCell_CellGroupDeleteReq (ID: 10966683)

**2.3.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12732215`)

Cell Group Delete

---

#### 2.3.2.2.0-8 Cell Group Delete PsCell_CellGroupDeleteResp (ID: 10966690)

**2.3.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12732217`)

Cell Group Delete
PsCell\_CellGroupDeleteResp message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| nrCellGrpId | [Before 5GC000998-A]0...127 [5GC000998-A]  0..3071 [End 5GC000998-A] | M | See 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5GC000718-N |

Note: messageResult is not needed since NOK reply not possible.

---

### 2.3.2.3 Cell Group Reconfiguration

#### 2.3.2.3.0-2 Cell Group Reconfiguration Overview (ID: 10966708)

**2.3.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12732221`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Messages:

PsCell\_CellGroupReconfigReq/Resp

Purpose:

To reconfigure the common parameters for cells of a NRCELLGRP (see 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Cell Group exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_100\_replaced([11178581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeZLUvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell Reconfiguration

---

#### 2.3.2.3.0-3 Cell Group Reconfiguration Description (ID: 10966713)

**2.3.2.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `10966725`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update the cell group context for the common on line modifiable parameters contained in the message and all related cell resources.

[Befor CB007490-C]The new values shall be valid for all (existing and new) UEs in the cells.[CB007490-C] For details of parameters applicability see parameters description.[End CB007490-C]

---

#### 2.3.2.3.0-4 Cell Group Reconfiguration Message Validation (ID: 10966729)

**2.3.2.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10966735`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellGroupReconfigReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupReconfigResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid, the cell group identified and reconfigured successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_7197\_replaced([10966753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQQLPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.3.0-5 Cell Group Reconfiguration Concurrency Handling (ID: 10966741)

**2.3.2.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10966747`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Concurrent Cell Group procedures are not managed at L2-RT side

If a Cell Group Reconfiguration procedure is initiated by 5G-CP-RT, no other Cell Group procedures (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated , until the on-going Cell Group Reconfiguration procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.3.0-6 Cell Group Reconfiguration Exceptions (ID: 10966753)

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `10966759`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Expected Exceptions

---

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10966764`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellGroupReconfigResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not reconfigured successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were reconfigured by the 5G-L2-PS.

---

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10966770`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Unexpected Exceptions

---

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10966776`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12649918`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
Handling of actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer for FR2 cells

---

**2.3.2.3.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12649920`)

Cell Group Reconfiguration
If the 5G-L2-PS receives a Cell Group Reconfiguration procedure for FR2 cells with actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer set to True, then 5G-L2-PS shall log an error message, ignore the actStatelessSchedLoadBalancer IE, and respond with PsCell\_CellGroupReconfigResp containing status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok.

---

### 2.3.2.4 Cell Setup

#### 2.3.2.4.0-2 Cell Setup Overview (ID: 10966860)

**2.3.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10966866`)

Cell Setup
Messages:

PsCell\_CellSetupReq/Resp

Purpose:

To setup a cell in 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Cell Group Setup is done

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_76\_replaced([11177702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeU55fvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell setup and L1 subcells setup

---

#### 2.3.2.4.0-3 Cell Setup Description (ID: 10966872)

**2.3.2.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10966877`)

Cell Setup
Overall information

---

**2.3.2.4.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10966883`)

Cell Setup
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall create the requested cell context, update the nrCellList for the cell group context, adding concerned cell. One L2-RT instance supports up to 8  NR cells.

[5GC000533-A] 5G-L2-PS shall add a new NRCELL object for PM, see 5G\_L2\_1517\_replaced([11192164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOzPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[5GC000523-D] Slot Pattern length rrmSlotPatternLength, along with resource allocations for CSI-RS and CSI reports (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2535) shall be included in the cell setup response message.

[5GC001804-A] For actions required for PCMD see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[5GC000679-B] actFdmScheduling added.

[5GC002537-A] actFdmEnhancedScheduling added. [End 5GC002537-A]

[5GC000399-KX] Flag actEcpriPhase2 is added in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, refer more to 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[5GC000399-Q] Flag actEcpriPhase3 is added in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, refer more to 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Structure prachOccasions is added in PsCell\_CellSetupResp for RU. refer more to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2341.

[FGCR-2646] structure dlSlotsBitMap is added in PsCell\_CellSetupResp. Refer more to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2302.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `10966889`)

Cell Setup
CA information

---

**2.3.2.4.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10966900`)

Cell Setup
For an FR1 CA enabled cell, the following information has to be included in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message:

- actInterNumerologyCa[5GC002546-A], flexibleCAMode[End 5GC002546-A]  (Feature activation control)

- crntiPoolId, maxNbOfCRNTIPools, crntiPoolConfig (C-RNTI pool information)

- caConfig (SCell activation / deactivation related parameters)

- [5GC002546-B]CellANPUCCHPool (PUCCH resource pool for Ack/Nack usage)[End 5GC002546-B]

---

#### 2.3.2.4.0-4 Cell Setup Message validation (ID: 10966906)

**2.3.2.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10966911`)

Cell Setup
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellSetupResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the cell was setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_59\_replaced([10966928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UReRvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.4.0-5 Cell Setup Concurrency handling (ID: 10966917)

**2.3.2.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10966923`)

Cell Setup
Concurrent Cell procedures are not managed at L2-RT side and for one Cell procedure, Cells shall be handle one after the other.

If a Cell Setup procedure is initiated for one cell by 5G-CP-RT toward L2-PS, L2-LO, no other Cell procedure (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated for any other Cell until this on-going Cell Setup procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.4.0-6 Cell Setup Exceptions (ID: 10966928)

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `10966934`)

Cell Setup
Generic handling

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-1.0-9**  (ID: `10966988`)

Cell Setup
Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) defines two types of exceptions, expected and unexpected.

Expected Exceptions:

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* nrCellGrpId IE is not known or;
* nrCellIdentity IE is not valid or it already exists or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not allocated successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Note: Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10966994`)

Cell Setup
MIMO specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10967001`)

Cell Setup
[Before CNI-89884-D] No functional changes, split from the previous version. [End CNI-89884-D]

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 and L2-PS failed to allocate cell specific CSI-RS resources in time domain (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2347), L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk and cause IE = NoUserPlaneResourcesAvailable.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `10967007`)

Cell Setup
**DSS Subframe reservation specific**

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10967013`)

Cell Setup
[Before CNI-89884-D] No functional changes, split from the previous version. [End CNI-89884-D]

If DSS Subframe reservations fails (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4716)   dedicated cause as 'DssSubframeReservationFailure together  with NOK status  shall be used.

'DssSubframeReservationFailure indicates that DSS Subframe Reservation procedure detects clashing of some resources (collision has been detected for SI/Paging or Msg2 reservation) and allows 5G-CP-RT to take appropriate action.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `12650616`)

Cell Setup
**Asymmetric DSS specific**

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12650619`)

Cell Setup
If actAsymmetricDss is TRUE:

* supported ul/dlBandwidth are 52, 79, 106,133,160, 188, 216, 270 PRBs

- lteNrSharedArea/endPrb - lteNrSharedArea/startPrb should be >= 50 PRBs (correspond to min LTE PRBs for 10MHz)

- cellBwp/longPucchStartPuschPrb and cellBwp/longPucchNumPuschPrb IE should be present and longPucch area should be within NR dedicated area

Otherwise 5G-L2-PS sends response with NOK status and cause IE = InvalidParameter.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-5**  (ID: `10967018`)

Cell Setup
Slice Aware Scheduler specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `10967036`)

Cell Setup
[Before CB008828-C]

5G-L2-PS sends response with NOK status and cause IE = InvalidParameter if at least one of the following rules is fulfilled:

* In case actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is disabled there is at least one PLMN with no configured slices and NSA resource group configuration absent (at least one slice or NSA resource group needs to be configured for each PLMN).
* In case actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled and there is a PLMN for which neither a slice nor nsaDefaultResourceGroupId is configured (at least one slice or nsaDefaultResourceGroupId needs to be configured for each PLMN).
* In case actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled and for the configured nsaDefaultResourceGroupId there is no resource group within resourceGroupList.
* In case actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is disabled, sum of number of slices among all PLMN's exceeds 20. Note NSA resource groups are not considered within these limitations.
* In case actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled, sum of number of slices among all PLMN's exceeds 20 or sum of slices plus number of resource groups in resourceGroupList exceeds 32.

5G-L2-PS sends response with NOK status and cause IE = InvalidParameter if sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true and at least one of the following rules is fulfilled:

* quotasConfig is not present for any slice or NSA resource group.
* minQuota within any slice or NSA resource group is out of range [0..100].
* maxQuota within any slice or NSA resource group is out of range [1..100].
* there is at least one slice or NSA resurce group where minQuota > maxQuota.
* sum of minQuotas in all slices and NSA resource groups is greater than 100.

Note. NSA resource group indicates:

* nsaResourceGroup parameter if actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is disabled,
* resourceGroup from resourceGroupList if actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled.

[CB008828-C][Before CB008709-A]

These checks are performed only when sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true:

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if resourceGroupConfig is not present.

[CB008709-A]Let's define set of resource group checks as (S1):[End CB008709-A]

* L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if there is at least one resource group or default resource group with id out of range configured in [Before CB008709-A]resourceGroupConfig[CB008709-A]resource group configuration[End CB008709-A].
* L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if there is more than one configuration for[Before CB008709-A] dl[End CB008709-A] resource group or[Before CB008709-A] dl[End CB008709-A] default resource group in [Before CB008709-A]resourceGroupConfig[CB008709-A]resource group configuration[End CB008709-A].

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if minQuota within any resource group is out of range [0..100].

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if maxQuota within any resource group is out of range [1..100].

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if there is at least one resource group where minQuota > maxQuota.

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if sum of minQuotas in all[Before CB008709-A] dl[End CB008709-A] resource groups is greater than 100.

* L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if there is at least one default resource group using unconfigured resource group.

[CB008709-A]If sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true:

 L2-PS sends response with NOK status and InvalidParameter(2) cause if dlResourceGroupConfig is not present.

 (S1) checks are performed for resource groups in dlResourceGroupConfig

If ulResourceGroupConfig is present then (S1) checks are performed for resource groups in ulResourceGroupConfig.[End CB008709-A]

[End CB008828-C]

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-6**  (ID: `10967042`)

Cell Setup
BfSetup

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `10967059`)

Cell Setup
5G-L2-PS should validate quarterSectorBeamPatternId when BfSetup is present and UL subCellType set as C8 or C8\_2 or C8\_4.

If the ul subCellType is C8 or C8\_2 or C8\_4 and quarterSectorBeamPatternId is absent, the 5G-L2-PS will report a negative acknowledgement in the PSCell\_CellSetupResp message with the following information:

-The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G\_NotOk);

-The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter);

with actEcpri72e = [Before CB009514-L] Ecpri72eUL or Ecpri72eULDL [CB009514-L] TRUE [End CB009514-L],  L2PS should validate the ULsubcelltype Cx\_y and numberOfRxPucch, if x≠ numberOfRxPucch , L2Ps will report a negative response -The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G\_NotOk);

-The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter)

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-7**  (ID: `10967066`)

Cell Setup
MU MIMO specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `10967072`)

Cell Setup
L2Ps shall check the configuration of ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch, only MCS compensation is supported when ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4.

L2Ps shall check the configuration of SE check which shall be disabled when ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4.

L2Ps shall check the actUlMuMimoGroupParing which shall be disabled when ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4.

Warning logs shall be printed if the check is failed.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-8**  (ID: `10967078`)

Cell Setup
PrbBlanking

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `10967083`)

Cell Setup
5G-L2-PS receives the configuration of the PrbBlanking in low and high edges for UL & DL.

In TDD

in case the configuration is invalid :

-number of Prbs blanked too high depending on the bandwidth or

-difference in the number of prbs blanked  in UL compared to DL

[CB009915-C] - RIM-RS config is not compatible with PRB Blanking Config. RIM-RS & Blanking configs are not compatible if, in rimRsConfig, for at least one startRbForRs,

startRbForRs < nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL OR

startRbForRs + numRbForRs  > total number of PRBs on the bandwidth -   nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

[End CB009915-C]

5G-L2-PS will report a negative acknowledgement in the PSCell\_CellSetupResp message with the following information:

-The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G\_NotOk);

-The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter);

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-10**  (ID: `10967102`)

Cell Setup
ZP-CSI-RS config specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `10967108`)

Cell Setup
FDD ZP-CSI-RS config exceptions

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-10.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13344852`)

Cell Setup
5G-L2-PS receives the configuration of ZP-CSI-RS in PsCell\_CellSetupReq as part of ZpCsiRsResource (5G\_L2\_IF\_6012\_replaced([10969296](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ub2Vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then L2-PS shall validate:

If *cellTechnology is set to FDD and* dss.nrLteDssMode set to None and ZpCsiRsAssocation is set to csiImOfFddNonDss, then:\*\*

**If  slowPrbPoolingAllowed = TRUE**

If (zpCsiRsConfig.*zpCsiRsConfig not equal to row4) Or (zpCsiRsConfig.*zpCsiRsfirstOFDMSymbolsInTimeDomain is set to value other than 4, 8 or 10), then:\*\*

5G-L2-PS will report a negative acknowledgement in the PSCell\_CellSetupResp message with the following information:

-The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G\_NotOk);

-The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter);

end

else

If (zpCsiRsConfig.*zpCsiRsConfig not equal to row4) Or (zpCsiRsConfig.*zpCsiRsfirstOFDMSymbolsInTimeDomain is set to value other than 7, 8, 9 or 12), then:\*\*

5G-L2-PS will report a negative acknowledgement in the PSCell\_CellSetupResp message with the following information:

-The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G\_NotOk);

-The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter);

end

end

end

[CB013525-D]

If *cellTechnology is set to FDD and dlMimoMode = 80 and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE, then*

ZpCsiRsAssocation is set to csiImOfFddBf8Port or csiImOfFddBf32Port(see [10969296: ZpCsiRsResource structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ub2Vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9));

zpCsiRsConfig.*zpCsiRsfirstOFDMSymbolsInTimeDomain shall be 4/8/10 for 8 port 4/7/8 for 32 port as per [11301928: CSI-IM with rate matching PDSCH in FDD non-DSS mode](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqdSIvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).*

end

[End CB013525-D]

Rationale: Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_685.

Notes:

* slowPrbPoolingAllowed is contained in PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq.L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations;
* CSI-IM Randomization is independent of L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations.slowPrbPoolingAllowed = TRUE and L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations.slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE.

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-11**  (ID: `10967136`)

Cell Setup
Artificial-load-specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `10967142`)

Cell Setup
Invalid patternId exception

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-11.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10967148`)

Cell Setup
Upon receiving the request message, 5G-L2-PS shall retrieve the patternIds configured for PDSCH for the given cell. This information shall be accessed from the bfSetup structure (5G\_L2\_IF\_115\_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is contained within the Fr1AggregatedSet structure (5G\_L2\_IF\_5475\_replaced([10969099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaoPPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which in turn is part of the Fr1Fr2Combined structure (5G\_L2\_IF\_5471\_replaced([10969086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaoOvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from PsCell\_CellSetupReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message content.

If any of the patternIds listed in the patternIdsForArtificialLoadForEmfTestMode list, which is part of the artificialLoadInfo structure (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_111\_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), cannot be found among the patternIds configured for PDSCH for the given cell, 5G-L2-PS shall generate a response with status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause = InvalidParameter (see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Rationale: Each target beam configured for DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation shall be a part of the existing set of beams allocated for PDSCH within the given cell.

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-12**  (ID: `12704898`)

Cell Setup
FDD Supercell specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `12704902`)

Cell Setup
Upon receiving the request message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the exception conditions as mentioned in [11142497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_hSqc8PvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-13**  (ID: `13409940`)

Cell Setup
PDCCH Specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `13409941`)

Cell Setup
Upon receiving a PsCell\_CellSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall validate the dciDedicatedAggregationLevel parameter.

If all the following conditions are met

1)In a [Before CB014330-SR-H-UPD001] K2 slot([11114685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB014330-SR-H-UPD001] possible K2 slot [End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001], If any of the configured Bandwidth Parts (BWP) other than initial BWP in cell setup has  dciDedicatedAggregationLevel  configured and provides only a single PDCCH occasion from all its UE-Specific Search Spaces (SS) combined.

2)The CORESET size corresponding to that single PDCCH occasion is smaller than 2 \* dciDedicatedAggregationLevel.

5G-L2-PS shall send a response message  PsCell\_CellSetupResp with   
the status IE set to NOK (EStatus5G\_NotOk) and   
the cause IE set to InvalidParameter (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter) and  
[CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
the needForRollback IE shall be set to true and   
[End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
a detailed diagnostic information for this failure as defined in [13359340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7tLkp_H3EfC0Z6kKit-MzQ).

Note:

[Before CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
K2 slots are identified based on the existing availableDlSlotsBitMapForK2Resources calculated upon cell setup request.  
[CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
The possible K2 slots are determined as follows:

* For TDD frame structures(1208, 1116, 1070) for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is supported, all DL/special slots that precede the next UL slot by up to k2rimMax([13432384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aDWAAx7VEfG-foklaHnAaA)).
* For TDD frame structures for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is not supported DL/Special slots that are rrmK2min slots ahead of UL slots([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
* For FDD, all DL slots shall be considered as K2 slots, even in a DSS cell.

[End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]

Validation of dciDedicatedAggregationLevel  parameter shall be done after existing validations of cellsetup  request are completed, to prioritize the critical faults.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-14**  (ID: `10967166`)

Cell Setup
Other feature specific

---

**2.3.2.4.0-6.0-14.0-5**  (ID: `12698162`)

Cell Setup
L2-PS sends response with NOK status and cause IE = InvalidParameter if at least one of the following rules is fulfilled:

* actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to pusch, pucchPusch, puschSrs or pucchPuschSrs but clpcPusch is missing in PsCell\_CellSetupReq,
* actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to pucch, pucchPusch or pucchPuschSrs but clpcPucch is missing in PsCell\_CellSetupReq,
* parameter maxNbOfCRNTIPools is not the same for all cells in an L2-PS instance,
* parameter crntiPoolId is not the same for all cells in a nrCellGroup,
* parameter crntiPoolId is the same for 2 different nrCellGroups,
* parameter crntiPoolId is equal or superior to maxNbOfCRNTIPools,
* all beams are muted: all bits in beamsMuted[0..numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks-1] range are set to 1,
* muted beams are out of allowed range (exceeds number of transmitted SSBs): at least one bit is set to 1 in beamsMuted[numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks..64] range,
* cellCsiRsLocation is present in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, time domain validation for CSI-RS resources in cellCsiRsLocation is failed (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9381). Detailed diagnostic information is defined in 5G\_L2\_6074\_replaced([11172623](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26XEhfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

for at least one of the entries in pdcchConfig.controlResourceSet, cceRegMappingType is set to 'interleaved' and interleaverRows is set to 'none'.

[Before CB010315-A]

* actNrRim is set to value other than "disabled" in **PsCell\_CellSetupReq** while any element of ulSubcellList contains eCpriFlag **= False**\*\*\*\*

[End CB010315-A]

* parameter actIncUlPdcchCapacity is True and structure dynPdcchTdMgt is not present

If ssBlockPower received in PsCell\_CellSetupReq **(5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is out of range, L2PS shall set the default value of MIN (-903) or MAX (0) depending on whether the received value out of the range is closer to MAX or MIN**.\*\*\*\*

**If enhCtrlChannelTransMode has value which is not defined as valid, then L2-PS shall set "TM\_Disabled" value.**

**[CB014054-G]**

* In case of Mixed Mode FH L2-PS send response with NOK status and Cause IE- ECause5G\_Undefined in following cases.
* When t5aMin and oneWayHwDelayDl both are present.
* When t5aMin and oneWayHwDelayDl both are absent.
* When t5aMin is configured in case of Cell technology TDD.
* When t5aMin is configured in case of frequency FR2.

[End CB014054-G]

#### 2.3.2.4.0-9 Cell Setup IE Definitions: (ID: 10967697)

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12825763`)

Cell Setup
**availablePucchAndCsiRsResources structure content**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| MaxSlotsPatternLength | 20..1280 |  |  | 5GC000523-D |
| availablePucchAndCsiRsResources [MaxSlotsPatternLength] |  |  |  | 5GC000523-D |
| >pucchResourceForCsiReport | u16 | O | The 14 bits bitmap where each bit is reserved to an OFDM symbol. Symbol 0 is mapped to the Least Significant Bit (LSB) of u16, symbol 13 is mapped to the (MSB - 2) of the u16.   The 15th bit, which is the (MSB - 1) of the u16, is set to 1 if the slot has PRACH. | 5GC000523-D |
| >csiRsResourcesInSsSlots | u16 | M | 14 bits bitmap where each bit is reserved to an OFDM symbol. Symbol 0 is mapped to the Least Significant Bit (LSB) of u16, symbol 13 is mapped to the (MSB - 2) of the u16.   If dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, last two symbols are reserved for CSIRS. Otherwise, only last one symbol is reserved for CSIRS in SSB slots   If {dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4  AND actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false} **OR {actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is true}** Or {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks < 5}, all bits of this IE shall be filled ‘0’.\*\*\*\*   If actPciBasedCsiImRandomization is set to ‘true`, L2PS shall set all symbols as unavailable. Please see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2363   If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks > 4, this IE will be filled by L2-PS and it is used by CP-RT to select UE specific CSI-RS resource.The symbols which can be used by UE specific CSI-RS resource refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2514. [CB008577-B]Note, for FDD BF (actBeamforming= True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80), L2PS will set all symbols as default value as 0 [End CB008577-B] | 5GC000523-D |
| >csiRsResourcesInDataSlots | u16 | M | 14 bits bitmap where each bit is reserved to an OFDM symbol. Symbol 0 is mapped to the Least Significant Bit (LSB) of u16, symbol 13 is mapped to the (MSB - 2) of the u16.   If {dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4  AND actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false} **OR {actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is true} Or {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks < 5}, all bits of this IE shall be filled ‘0’.**   If actPciBasedCsiImRandomization is set to ‘true`, L2PS shall set one symbol per SSB periodicity.  Otherwise all symbols are unavailable. Please see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2363.   If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks > 4, this IE will be filled by L2-PS and it is used by CP-RT to select UE specific CSI-RS resource.The symbols which can be used by UE specific CSI-RS resource refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2530. [CB008577-B]Note, for FDD BF (actBeamforming= True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80), L2PS will set all symbols as default value as 0 [End CB008577-B] | 5GC000523-D |
| >goldenPucchResourcesForCsiReport | u16 | O | 14 bits bitmap where each bit is reserved to an OFDM symbol. Symbol 0 is mapped to the Least Significant Bit (LSB) of u16, symbol 13 is mapped to the (MSB - 2) of the u16.   Pucch Resources that should be granted in priority to RRC connected users compared to regular Pucch Resources | 5GC001127-B |

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `10967736`)

prachOccasions structure content

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `12978335`)

Cell Setup
**prachOccasions structure content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| patternLengthPrach | 1, 2, 4,  8, 16 | M | PRACH occasions repetition pattern length, expressed as a number of 10 ms radio frame. Pattern start is aligned with start of the radio frame with SFN # 0. | 5GC000399-Q |
| subCarrierSpacing | Enum { kHz1p25, kHz5, kHz15, kHz30, kHz60, kHz120 } | M | Subcarrier spacing (SCS) of the PRACH occasions. Note:  Value kHz30 or kHz15 for TDD FR1, **see note 3.** Value kHz1p25 is used for PRACH preamble format 0 **and format 1.**\*\*\*\* | 5GC000399-Q |
| frequencyOffset | -78624…76896 , step 1 | M | Offset of center frequency of lowest-frequency PRACH RE in lowest-frequency PUSCH PRB occupied by all the PRACH occasions of the cell/carrier from center frequency of UL cell/carrier, expressed as a number of half PRACH REs | 5GC000399-Q |
| gtLowBandwidth | 1, 2, 7, 10, 12, 133 | M | In lowest-frequency PUSCH PRBs occupied by one PRACH occasion, number of PRACH guard tones / PRACH guard REs before lowest-frequency non-guard RE of the PRACH occasion.  Refer 3GPP 38.211, Table 6.3.3.2-1. Note:  Always value 2 for TDD FR1 for now, see note 3. Value 1 is used for PRACH preamble format 0**.  Value 7 for FDD FR1 is used for PRACH preamble format 0** and format 1**.**\*\*\*\* | 5GC000399-Q |
| prachBandwidth | 139, 839 | M | Number of PRACH non-guard REs of one PRACH occasion. Note:  Always value 139 for TDD FR1 for now, see note 3. **Value 839 is used for PRACH preamble format 0** and format 1.\*\*\*\* | 5GC000399-Q |
| gtHighBandwidth | 3, 13, 15, 18, 24, 180 | M | In highest-frequency PUSCH PRBs occupied by one PRACH occasion, number of PRACH guard tones / PRACH guard REs after highest-frequency non-guard RE of the PRACH occasion. Note:  Always value 3 for TDD FR1 for now, see note 3. Value 24 is used for PRACH preamble format 0. Value 18 for FDD FR1 is used for PRACH preamble format 0 **and format 1.** | 5GC000399-Q |
| cpDuration | 1080...840960 step 1 | M | Cyclic Prefix length of the PRACH occasion, expressed in UTU (1 / 1.2288GHz = ~0.813802ns). Refer to 3GPP 38.211, Table 6.3.3.1-1 and Table 6.3.3.1-2. Note:  Only values 11520, 18720 or 40960 **or 81920** for TDD FR1 for now, see note 3**. Value 126720 is used for PRACH preamble format 0,and value 840960 is used for PRACH preamble format 1.**\*\*\*\* | 5GC000399-Q |
| sequenceDuration | 10240...983040 step 1 | M | Length of the PRACH preamble sequence contained in one PRACH occasion, expressed in UTU (1 / 1.2288GHz = ~0.813802ns). Refer to 3GPP 38.211, Table 6.3.3.1-1 and Table 6.3.3.1-2. Note:  Always value 40960 or 81920 **for TDD FR1 for now, see note 3.** Value 983040 is used for PRACH preamble format 0 **and format 1.**\*\*\*\* | 5GC000399-Q |
| sequenceRepetitions | 1, 2, 4, 6,8, 9, 10, 11,  12 | M | Number of repetitions of the PRACH preamble sequence contained in one PRACH occasion. Refer to 3GPP 38.211, Table 6.3.3.1-1 and Table 6.3.3.1-2.   Note:  Only values 4 or 12 for TDD FR1 are supported, **unless addExtDelayCompensation is set to value different than 0.0. In that case sequenceRepetitions can be set to values between 8..12 depending on the addExtDelayCompensation parameter value.** (see note 3)***\* Value 1 is used for PRACH preamble format 0* \*and value 2 is used for PRACH format 1.** | 5GC000399-Q |
| prachOccasionsList | [1...24] | M | List of PRACH occasions positions in time and in frequency over the PRACH pattern duration. Note:  Limited to max. 24 for TDD FR1 for now, see notes 1 and 2. In case of supercell PRACH occasions shall be listed in order of ulSubcellList entries in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, see note 4. | 5GC000399-Q |
| > timeOffset | 0...196607999   step 1 (equivalent to from 0ms, included, to 160ms, not included) | M | Time offset of the start of the Cyclic Prefix of the PRACH occasion from start of the slot # 0 at start of the PRACH pattern, expressed in UTU (1 / 1.2288GHz = ~0.813802ns). Does not include impact from NTAoffset.   It includes shift caused by PsCell\_CellSetupReq.addExtDelayCompensation parameter value != 0.0. Please see 5G\_L2\_13498\_replaced([11157464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25F5NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details. | 5GC000399-Q |
| >reOffset | 0...8064   step 1 | M | Frequency offset of the lowest-frequency PRACH RE in lowest-frequency PUSCH PRB occupied by the here considered PRACH occasion from lowest-frequency PRACH RE in lowest-frequency PUSCH PRB occupied by all the PRACH occasions of the cell/carrier, expressed as a number of PRACH REs. | 5GC000399-Q |
| >beamListMPlane | [1...4] | M | List of structures including patternId and list of ceAxCIds associated with related beam for the PRACH occasion or in case of supercell with related L1 subcell for the PRACH occasion, see note 4. The number of element could be 1, 2, 3, or 4. | 5GC002244-A |
| >>patternId | 0...32767 step 1 | O | patternId of beam applied to the PRACH occasion. Optional IE. Only value 0 in case of supercell. In case of ULA Cell with 1 SSB (see [13256670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UInXtMlGEfCYBIz6acpPHw)) halfSectorBeamPatternId shall be used. | 5GC002244-A |
| >>ceAxCIdList | u16 [1...4] | M | List of ceAxCId to be used for the given beam on eCPRI fronthaul or in case of supercell list of ceAxCId to be used for the given virtual beam associated with L1 subcell, see note 4. | 5GC002244-A |

Note 1: refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2341 for more detail information.

Note 2:  The structure “prachOccasions” is not ready for support, if/when needed in the future, of:

* PRACH configuration index values for combined PRACH preamble formats A1/B1, A2/B2 or A3/B3, or
* contention-free random access, contention-free beam failure recovery or SI request via random access using different PRACH configuration index, PRACH positions in frequency or PRACH SCS than the “basis” PRACH configuration index, PRACH positions in frequency and PRACH SCS defined for the 5G cell in the RRC IE “RACH-ConfigCommon” or in the therein contained RRC IE “RACH-ConfigGeneric”.

Note 3:  For TDD FR1 for now, PUSCH SCS is 30 kHz and used PRACH formats would/could be A2, B4 or C2, all with PRACH SCS of also 30 kHz for A2,B4 format, or with PRACH SCS of 30 kHz or 15kHz for C2 format. For TDD FR1, PRACH preamble format 0 is also supported with PRACH SCS is 1.25kHz.

Whena addExtDelayCompensation is set to value different than 0.0 then only B4 PRACH configurations are expected and number of repetitions provided to 5G-CP-RT are adapted based on the time shift of PRACH caused by addExtDelayCompensation delay value. See 5G\_L2\_13498\_replaced([11157464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25F5NvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) regarding the detailed explanation of timeOffsetMPlane and sequenceRepetitionsMPlane calculations.

Note 4:

For supercell (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) L2-PS shall ensure N-th entry of prachOccasionList connects to N-th entry of ulSubcellList (5G\_L2\_IF\_77\_replaced([10968024](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVvvfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and thus PRACH occasions are mapped to corresponding L1 subcells/virtual beams (beam IDs) of supercell. See 5G\_UP\_1851\_replaced([11375846](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLIfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details of ulSubcellList entries/beam IDs mapping.

[CB008577-A]

Note 5: When FDD beamforming UL subcell A8, number of PRACH steam is 4 (see [11388574: Mapping table between ulSubcellType (L1 BU) and number of spatial streams in CPRI and eCPRI 7-2a](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxNPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))when actPrachProbing = FALSE but only one sector beam is for PRACH receiving, so beamListMPlane will filled with 2 elements, in the 2 elements the patternId shall be the same and in each element ceAxCIdList shall be filled with a half of the 4 streams.  If actPrachProbing = TRUE, number of PRACH steam for A8 UL subcell is 8, so beamListMPlane will filled with 4 elements with different UL patternId from beam set4 and in each element ceAxCIdList shall be filled with a 1/4 of the 8 streams.

[End CB008577-A]

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7**  (ID: `10967885`)

Cell Setup
Parameter Details

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `10967891`)

Cell Setup
ulSubcellCaps

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `10967902`)

Cell Setup
UL Subcell Capabilities

Indicates UL subcell channel capacity at L2-PS level. Parameter is relevant only for cmWave as in mmWave each subcell support all channels.

Bitmap with following range:

{0x00000000 ... 0x00000007}

Bitmap with following values:

SUBCELL\_CAP\_PUCCH             0x00000001

SUBCELL\_CAP\_PUSCH             0x00000002

SUBCELL\_CAP\_RACH               0x00000004

It is a bitmap of different bitmask values which means that:

- value 0x00000000 indicates that any defined channel (PUCCH, PUSCH, RACH) is not used by the subcell.

- value 0x00000001 indicates that only PUCCH is used by the subcell.

- …

-     value 0x00000007 indicates that all defined channels (PUCCH, PUSCH, RACH) is used by the subcell.

Note:

* SU MIMO SRS follows the PUSCH capability

[5GC001086-A] -Periodic SRS scheduling only apply to primary subcell, i.e. subcell with value 0x00000007 [End 5GC001086-A]

* Please refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_69\_replaced([10967933](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVIr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail value of ulSubcellCaps in different subcell deployment scenarios.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `10967908`)

Cell Setup
dlSubcellCaps

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10967915`)

Cell Setup
DL Subcell Capabilities

Indicates DL subcell channel capacity at L2-PS level.

Parameter is relevant only in case of cmWave as in mmWave each subcell supports all channels and because of that parameter can get any value from value range in mmWave (analog BF) configurations.

Bitmap with following range:

{0x00000000 ... 0x000000FF}

Bitmap with following bitmask value:

SUBCELL\_CAP\_CSIRS\_REF       0x00000001

SUBCELL\_CAP\_CSIRS\_CPR       0x00000002

SUBCELL\_CAP\_CSIRS\_TRS       0x00000004

SUBCELL\_CAP\_SSB                  0x00000008

SUBCELL\_CAP\_PDCCH              0x00000010

SUBCELL\_CAP\_PDSCH              0x00000020

It is a bitmap of different bitmask values which means that:

- value 0x00000000 indicates that CSI-RS ref, CSI-RS cpr, CSI-RF trs, SSB, PDCCH and PDSCH are not used by the subcell.

- value 0x00000001 indicates that CSI-RS for beam refinment is used by the subcell.

- value 0x00000002 indicates that CSI-RS CQI/PMI/RI is used by the subcell.

- value 0x00000004 indicates that CSI-RS for tracking is used by the subcell.

-     value 0x00000008 indicates that SSB is used by the subcell.

-     value 0x00000010 indicates that PDCCH is used by the subcell.

-     value 0x00000020 indicates that PDSCH is used by the subcell.

-     value 0x000000FF indicates that all defined channels (CSI-RS ref, CSI-RS cpr, CSI-RS trs, SSB, PDCCH and PDSCH) are used by the subcell.

Note: Please refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_69\_replaced([10967933](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVIr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail value of dllSubcellCaps in different subcell deployment scenarios.

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `10967921`)

Cell Setup
CellTechnology

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10967927`)

Cell Setup
5G-L2-PS can distinguish between TDD and FDD based on the cellTechnology received via PsCell interface.

Note:  There is no specific check of UE capabilities between FDD vs TDD. This should be handled in a feature development.

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `10967933`)

Cell Setup
ulSubcellCaps and dlSubcellCaps in different subcell deployment scenarios

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-7.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `10967958`)

Cell Setup
Details of channel supported per subcells in NrCellType definition tables

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Deployment scenario | DL Supported channels per subcells | dlSubcellCaps | UL Supported channels per subcells | ulSubcellCaps | Applicable to eCPRI (\*) |
| Scenario A: one DL and UL subcells per cell | All DL channels | 0xFF | All UL channels | 0x7 | YES |
| Scenario B: More than one DL subcell per cells with digital beamforming | [\*]Primary Subcell: SSB, CSI-RS, PDCCH, PDSCH Secondaries subcells: PDCCH, PDSCH | [\*]Primary Subcell: 0xFF   Secondaries subcells: 0x30 | NA | NA | YES |
| Scenario C: More than one UL subcell per cells with digital beamforming | NA | NA | [\*]Primary Subcell: PRACH, PUCCH, PUSCH, SRS   Secondaries subcells: PUCCH, PUSCH, SRS | [\*]Primary Subcell: 0x7   Secondaries subcells: 0x3 | Loner: YES Loki: NO [CB009028-5G-G] Thor: YES [End CB009028-5G-G] |
| Scenario D: More than one DL subcelltype C2 per cells with digital beamforming (this scenario is 2DL\*2UL inherited from 5G19B) | [\*]Primary Subcell: SSB, CSI-RS (cpr/trs), PDCCH, PDSCH Secondaries subcells: CSI-RS(ref/trs) | [\*]Primary Subcell: 0x3E   Secondaries subcells: 0x05 |  |  | NO |
| Scenario E: More than one DL subcell and UL subcell per supercell without beamforming. Note that all subcells are considered as primary subcells. | All DL channels | 0xFF | All UL channels | 0x7 | Loner: NO Loki: YES [CB009028-5G-G] Thor: YES [End CB009028-5G-G] |

Note:

[\*]Primary subcell refers:

* At L2 the subcell with the lowest bfcmIndex Value. [5G\_L2\_IF\_75\_replaced([10967982](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVvtvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_L2\_IF\_77\_replaced([10968024](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVvvfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

Column (\*) indicates which nrCellType deployment rules are also extended to eCpri. Loki is the board to be considered, Loner is only given as information. When no indication, it is same for both.

Only in TDD FR1 eCpri for Loki and vDU, static mapping are no more used to select number and subcells subcellType (CP3 impacts). For other cases, static mapping table are still used at OAM implementation step.

Important Note: This requirement only specify the detail value of column dlSubcellCaps and ulSubcellCaps in different subcell deployment scenarios, the rest parts shall be mirrored from 5G\_UP\_2554\_replaced([11390916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufWXWfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `10967976`)

Cell Setup
resourceRegionsForPrbFragmentation struct parameters

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| longPucchStartSr1Prb | 0...272 , step 1 | PUCCH SR resource start PRB region 1 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchStartSr2Prb | 0...272 , step 1 | PUCCH SR resource start PRB region 2 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchStartHarq1Prb | 0...272, step 1 | PUCCH HARQ resource start PRB region 1 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchStartHarq2Prb | 0...272 , step 1 | PUCCH HARQ resource start PRB region 2 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchStartPcsi1Prb | 0...272 , step 1 | PUCCH pCSI resource start PRB region 1 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchStartPcsi2Prb | 0...272 , step 1 | PUCCH pCSI resource start PRB region 2 | CB008941-A |
| longPucchNumSrPrb | 1...137 , step 1 | Number of SR PRB's reserved | CB008941-A |
| longPucchNumHarqPrb | 1...137 , step 1 | Number of Harq PRB's reserved | CB008941-A |
| longPucchNumPcsiPrb | 1...137 , step 1 | Number of Pcsi PRB's allocated | CB008941-A |

As per 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9180\_replaced([11310801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrS_rfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

longPucchNumSrPrb = #PRB(SR) /2

longPucchNumHarqPrb = #PRB(HARQ AN)/2

longPucchNumPcsiPrb = k\*#PRB(pCSI)/2

[CB009915-C]   
if (nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL>0)

LongPucchStartSr1Prb, longPucchStartHarq1Prb and longPucchStartPcsi1Prb  shall be greater or equal to nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL.

nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL is the number of blanked prb at low edge.

if it is not true, a log\_err is generated and a cellSetup ko is returned to CPRT.  
endif

if (nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL>0)  
    (longPucchStartSr2Prb+longPucchNumSrPrb), (longPucchStartHarq2Prb+longPucchNumHarqPrb) and (longPucchStartPcsi2Prb+longPucchNumPcsiPrb)

shall be lower than (ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL).

nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeULis the number of blanked prb at high edge.

if it is not true, a log\_err is generated and a cellSetup ko is returned to CPRT.  
endif

[End CB009915-C]

| firstPdcchMonitoringOccasionOfPo[ns] | 0...17919 | first PDCCH monitoring occasion of each paging occasion in the paging frame; Ref. pcch-Config in 38.331 for details.   The size of the parameter is the number of paging occasion per paging frame ns. The range of entries for the parameter is based on combination of subcarrier spacing and the number of total paging frames in a paging cycle n.   NOTE: The value provided in NIDD is OFDM symbol index within one radio frame. At User Plane it will get slot index within a radio frame = floor(firstPDCCH-MonitoringOccasionOfPO/14). | 5GC000733-F 5GC002063-A |

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `10968328`)

Cell Setup
[5GC000742-H] Not valid from this onwards.

This structure is replaced by cellBwp structure (5G\_L2\_IF\_95\_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which configures all bandwidth parts, including initial BWP, in the cell.

initialBwp structure content:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-20.0-6**  (ID: `12570518`)

Cell Setup
**tddFrameStructure content:**

The tddFrameStructure is a data type which is used for multiple (optional) elements within the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message**.**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| [Before CNI-134395-AA] isFrameStructureFlexible [End CNI-134395-AA] | TRUE, FALSE | M | Indicates whether Flexible Frame Structure is applicable (ie 5GC000542) Set to TRUE if MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL.tddFrameStructure. tddFrameStructureType = flexible. Set to FALSE if MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL.tddFrameStructure. tddFrameStructureType = {semiStatic}   Set to FALSE if MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL.tddFrameStructure. tddFrameStructureType = tdLte. |  |
| ulDlDataSlotRatio | enum { 1="1\_9\_ratio", 2="2\_8\_ratio", 3="3\_7\_ratio", 4="5\_5\_ratio", 5="1\_4\_ratio", 6="4\_6\_ratio", **[CB008453-A]** 7="4\_4\_ratio", **[End CB008453-A]** 32="6\_4\_ratio" } | M | Ratio of DL / UL logical data NR-slots used in the dynamic NR-slot selection algorithm. [Before CNI-134395-AA] Valid if isFrameStructureFlexible = TRUE [End CNI-134395-AA] | 5GC000542-A |
| semiStaticFrameStructure | A structure | M | [Before CNI-134395-AA] Valid if isFrameStructureFlexible = FALSE [End CNI-134395-AA] | 5GC001127-B 5GC001116-B |
| >patternOffset | 0..9 slots | M | Number of slots to offset the start of interfering pattern relative to slot 0 of the used tddFrameStructure. Used to correctly align a tdLte frame with 3ms shift when configured as either own frame structure or interfering frame structure. | 5GC002516-A |
| >referenceScs | Enum {15kHz, 30kHz, 60kHz, 120kHz, 240kHz} | M | 120kHz for FR2 30kHz for FR1 | 5GC001127-B |
| >gpLengt | Enum {1,2,4,6,10, 3, 5, 7} **symbols** | M | Number of Guard Symbols {2,6,10} are supported in FR2 {2,4,6} are supported in FR1 {10} is supported in FR1 {3,5,7} are supported in FR1 and used when PsCell\_CellSetupReq.addExtDelayCompensation is set to other value than 0 | 5GC001127-B |
| >Pattern1 | A structure | M | Provides the UL/DL symbols direction of Pattern1 length slots in a pattern of (Pattern1 length + Pattern 2 length) slots. Pattern1 defines gpLength guard symbols from starting position gpStartSymbol in gpStartOffset slot. All symbols prior to the guard period in Pattern1 are DL, all symbols after the guard period in Pattern1 are UL | 5GC001127-B |
| >>patternLength | 1..160 slots | M | If only Pattern1 is configured, patternLength must divide 20ms = 20*2^referenceScs. {5, 6, [**CB008453-A] 8,* *[End CB008453-A]10} slots is supported*\*\*\* |  |
| >>gpStartOffset | 0..159 | M | Slot position in pattern 1 of the first guard symbol. {3, 7} is supported |  |
| >>gpStartSymbol | 0..13 | M | Position of the first guard symbol in the slot positioned at gpStartOffset in the pattern1 {2, 4, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10} are supported. |  |
| >Pattern2 | A structure | M | Provides the UL/DL symbols direction of Pattern2 length slots in a pattern of (Pattern1 length + Pattern 2 length) slots. Pattern2 defines gpLength guard symbols from starting position gpStartSymbol in gpStartOffset slot. All symbols prior to the guard period in Pattern2 are DL, all symbols after the guard period in Pattern2 are UL | 5GC001116-B 5GC001070-B |
| >>patternLength | 0..160 slots | M | If only Pattern1 is configured, patternLength = 0. Pattern1 patternLength + Pattern2 patternLength must divide 20ms = 20\*2^referenceScs. {4, 5} is supported |  |
| >>gpStartOffset | 0..160 | M | Slot position in pattern2 of the first guard symbol If Pattern2 only contains DL symbols, then gpStartOffset = patternLength. {2, 4} is supported |  |
| >>gpStartSymbol | 0..13 | M | Position of the first guard symbol in the slot positioned at gpStartOffset in the pattern2. Not applicable if gpStartOffset = patternLength. {8,10} is supported |  |

| actDlRankProbing | TRUE, FALSE | M | Activation flag for the rank 4 probing for sounding based beamforming. If NRCELL.actDlRankProbing is equal to TRUE, then both NRCELL.actDlSrsBm and NRCELL.actInterRankSwitchBlock shall be equal to TRUE.   See definition of NIDD parameters NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlRankProbing   Note: This CNI is released to Customer via CB012783 with the scope not changed. | CNI-110468 |
| actDlLaEnhCqi2McsTables | Boolean | M | Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/ actDlLaEnhCqi2McsTables. If set as TRUE, then activates the 3GPP based CQI to MCS mapping tables in DL Link Adaptation (see 5G\_UP\_13335\_replaced([11363931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udGUmvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_13535\_replaced([11163458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25mPj_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). | CNI-124764 |
| actDlForceRankDowng | ENUMERATED {disabled: 0; dlVoNROnly:1; dlSRBOnly:2; dlVoNRCtrlOnly  :3; dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrl:4; dlNonGbrBrOnly: 5; dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr:6} | M | Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/actDlForceRankDowng. If set as 5, then activates the mechanism of Forced Rank Downgrade at Low CQI and High BLER (see 5G\_L2\_22721\_replaced([11164116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25qg__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If set as value other than 0 or 5, then activates the mechanism of DL Forced Rank Downgrade of transmissions with only VoNR 5QI1 (dlVoNROnly), only SRB(dlSRBOnly), only 5QI5 (dlVoNRCtrl) both VoNR 5QI1 ,SRB  and/or 5QI5(dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrl), and/or VoNR 5QI1 and/or SRB and/or 5QI5 and/or nonGBR with basic reliability for FDD (dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr) and controls the max MCS as per dlForceRankDowngCtl structure. Default value is 0. | CNI-135068 |
| shortTermBlerThreshold1 | uint8 [0..100] | O | Only present if *actDlForceRankDowng IE is set to 5. Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/shortTermBlerThreshold1.* It indicates PDSCH BLER threshold to enter rank downgrade state (see 5G\_L2\_22721\_replaced([11164116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25qg__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Default values is 12. | CNI-135068 |
| shortTermBlerThreshold2 | uint8 [0..100] | O | Only present if *actDlForceRankDowng IE is set to 5. Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/shortTermBlerThreshold2.* It indicates PDSCH BLER threshold to exit rank downgrade state (see 5G\_L2\_22721\_replaced([11164116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25qg__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Default values is 10. | CNI-135068 |
| deltaCqiOffsetAdjHo | uint8 [0..15] | M | Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/deltaCqiOffsetAdjHo. This parameter is used to set/unset additional delta CQI offset adjustment upon incoming handover (see 5G\_L2\_22725\_replaced([11163689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25oEufvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If set as 0, then the mechanism is deactivated. Default value is 0. | CNI-135068 |
| seThrTargetBlerReduct | uint16 [0..290] | M | Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/seThrTargetBlerReduct. This parameter is used to set/unset threshold for target BLER reduction at cell edge (see 5G\_L2\_22727\_replaced([11163698](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25oEu_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The NIDD’s value is multiplied by 10 for interface purposes, e.g. 28.9 sent as 289. If set as 0, then the mechanism is deactivated. Default value is 0. | CNI-135068 |
| targetBlerReductFactor | uint8 [0..10] | O | Only present if *seThrTargetBlerReduct IE is set to different value than 0. Value shall be set according to NIDD parameter NRCELL/targetBlerReductFactor.* It is used for target BLER adjustment, according to 5G\_L2\_22727\_replaced([11163698](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25oEu_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The NIDD’s value is multiplied by 10 for interface purposes, e.g. 0.8 sent as 8. Default value is 8 (which is equivalent to NIDD’s 0.8). | CNI-135068 |
| dlForceRankDowngCtl | Structure | O | Present only when actDlForceRankDowng set to dlSRBOnly, dlVoNRCtrlOnly, dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrl, or dlVonrSrbVoNRCtrNonGbrBr. | CB009849-C |
| > maxMcsForDlSrb | uint8 [0..28] | M | Limits the maximum MCS used for SRB1/2. Default Value is 19. |  |
| > maxMcsForDlVonrCtrl | uint8 [0..28] | M | Limits the maximum MCS used for 5QI5. Default value is 19. |  |
| dlLaCorrImpForDowngradedMcsAck | uint8 [0..200] | M | If the value of this parameter is different from 0, then the ACK of DL transmissions with downgraded MCS is used in OLLA algorithm | [CB015683-A] |
| dlLaAvgCqiFilterConst | [1..100] step 1 | M | Filter constant of the exponential filter for basic reliability. Default value is 1. | [CNI-164101] |
| mcsDowngradeMaxReduction | [0...28] step 1 | M | Maximum MCS reduction allowed when performing a DL MCS downgrade. Default value: 28 | 05601742 |

Except above parameters received from 5G-CP-RT, 5G-L2-PS could use its own hardcoded priorities for other UE’s activities.

E.g. *systemInformation broadcasts -> prio=101*

*paging broadcasts -> prio=100*

For more info, see [Before CB015279-A] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9891 [CB015279-A] [11174018: Full list of TD resource request class priorities](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB015279-A]

| Parameter |  | Range |  | Optionality |  | Description |  | First Feature |  |  |
|  | mcsIndex |  | 0...28 |  | M |  | Defines the MCS used for artificial load generation. 256QAM is not supported, so MCS index table defined in table 5.1.3.1-1 in 38.214 is used.   [CB010944-A] Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/mcsIndexForArtificialLoad [End CB010944-A] |  | 5GC000526-A |  |
|  | totalLoad |  | 0 … 100%, step 1% |  | M |  | Defines the target PDSCH load (artificial) [CB010944-A] for artificial load generation for DL performance testing [End CB010944-A] in percent for the empty slot in cell. Values from range 0-100 are allowed with step 1. 0 indicates that no artificial load is needed.   [CB010944-A] Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/targetTotalLoad [End CB010944-A] |  | 5GC000526-A |  |
|  | actConfDlInterferenceGen |  | Enum { 0:none, 1:PDSCH, 2:PDSCH+PDCCH, 3:PDSCH+PDCCH+TRS+SSB } |  | M |  | This parameter activates/deactivates the configurable DL interference generation over sector beam.   This parameter indicates also the type of DL artificial load to generate in the cell: - 'none' means deactivated - 'PDSCH' means generating artificial load on PDSCH slots only - 'PDSCH+PDCCH' means generating artificial load on PDSCH and PDCCH slots only - 'PDSCH+PDCCH+TRS+SSB' means generating artificial load on PDSCH and PDCCH slots, including PDSCH and PDCCH symbols on TRS and SSB slot   Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/actConfDlInterferenceGen |  | CB010944-A |  |
|  | targetTotalLoadSectorBeam |  | 0 … 100 %, step 1% |  | O |  | This parameter indicates the target total load (normal + artificial load) for creating artificial load in the cell. The artificial load is created using the sector beam and covers whole cell.   \* When normal load is below the target load, the artificial load is added up to the target load. \* When normal load is greater than or equal to the target load, no artificial load is added.   When this IE is not present, 5G-L2-PS shall internally set targetTotalLoadSectorBeam to 0. If targetTotalLoadSectorBeam is equal to 0, then no artificial load shall be created in the given cell.   Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/targetTotalLoadSectorBeam |  | CB010944-A |  |
|  | patternIdsForArtificialLoadForEmfTestMode |  | List of from 0 to 5 entries |  | M |  | This list controls DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation.  To disable the test mode for EMF validation, the size of this list shall be set to zero.  To enable the test mode for EMF validation, at least one target beam shall be set via this list. If multiple beams are configured, 5G-L2-PS shall randomly select one of these beams in the given PDSCH slot.   Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/actEmfTestMode |  | CB010944-A |  |
|  | >patternId |  | 0 … 2^16 - 1 |  | M |  | This parameter indicates the pattern ID of a target beam for EMF test mode. |  | CB010944-A |  |
|  | emfTargetTotalLoad |  | 0 … 100 %, step 1% |  | O |  | This parameter indicates the target total load (normal + artificial load) for creating artificial load in the cell for EMF test mode. The artificial load is created using the selected beams (see patternIdsForArtificialLoadForEmfTestMode).   \* When normal load is below the target load, the artificial load is added up to the target load. \* When normal load is greater than or equal to the target load, no artificial load is added.   When this IE is not present, 5G-L2-PS shall internally set emfTargetTotalLoad to 0. If emfTargetTotalLoad is equal to 0, then no artificial load shall be created in the given cell.   Configured by the NIDD parameter: NRBTS/NRCELL/emfTargetTotalLoad |  | CB010944-A |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

[CB010944-A]

|  |  |  |  |  |

| numberOfCellSegments | 1..60 | M | numberOfCellSegments to monitor and control EIRP. In case of TDD [CB009543-C1] or FDD [End CB009543-C1] supercell (NRCELL.actSupercell = true) numberOfCellSegments = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells | 5GC001329-A |
| maxBeamGain | 0..50 dBi per 0.1 step | M | Correspond to Gmlb for EIRP measurements. In the case of sector beam, corresponds to boresight beam gain. In the case of GoB BF, corresponds to the maximum achievable gain used as a normalization factor | 5GC001329-A |
| maxBeamGainForNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving | 0..50 dBi per 0.1 step | O | Additional *maxBeamGain value for reducedEnergySaving mode. Only needed when cell is a subject for massive MIMO muting for energy efficiency (see 5G\_L3\_15819\_replaced([11022741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Upnf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))).* | CB008133-B |
| normalizedBeamGain[] | uint16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | M | For each beam, normalized beam gain per cell segment shall be provided in Q1.15 linear scale. 1 value corresponds to maxBeamGain   The list size: – minimum is 1, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT where:   MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM = 64, MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT = 60 In case of TDD [CB009543-C1] or FDD [End CB009543-C1] supercell (NRCELL.actSupercell = true), The list size: – minimum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM*2, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell     CP-RT fills the first "numberOfBeamsInSupercell \* numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell " number of elements of the list with valid values. Rest of the elements are filled with 0.   where,   MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM = 64,   numberOfBeamsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells,   numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells | 5GC001329-A |
| normalizedBeamGainForNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving[] | uint16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | O | Additional *normalizedBeamGain values for reducedEnergySaving mode. Only needed when cell is a subject for massive MIMO muting for energy efficiency (see 5G\_L3\_15819\_replaced([11022741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Upnf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))).* | CB008133-B |
| powerReductionFactor[] | int16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | M | power reduction factor to determine maximum normalized EIRP over timeAveragingWindow Allowed range of values is -25...0 [dB] per 0.1 [dB] step Note: int16 value must be divided by 10 to obtain a step of 0.1 The list size: – minimum is 1, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT = 60   In case of TDD [CB009543-C1] or FDD [End CB009543-C1] supercell (NRCELL.actSupercell = true) The list size: – minimum is 2, – maximum is numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell   CP-RT fills the first "numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell" number of elements of the list with valid values.   where, numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells | 5GC001329-E |
| eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow | 1..30 minutes | M | Sliding window size for EIRP control   The step of the sliding window is define by eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize   A maximum of 3600 samples per window is supported (for example 6 minutes with 100ms sampling period or 30 minutes with 500ms sampling period)) | 5GC001329-E |
| eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize | 100..1000 ms per 20ms step | M | Sampling period for EIRP measurements and EIRP control sliding window step size   eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize must divide eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow | 5GC002300-C |
| minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode | Enum {actualEirpBudgetRatio, maxPowerBudgetRatio} | M | defines the mode applicable for the minimum guaranteed budget ratio of EIRP control | 5GC002300-D |
| minGuaranteedBudgetRatio | 0..1 per 0.01 step | M | defines the minimum guaranteed budget that shall be available in any EIRP control window step size.   If minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode is configured to actualEirpBudgetRatio then minGuaranteedBudgetRatio is relative to the power reduction factor of each cell segment.   If minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode is configured to maxPowerBudgetRatio then minGuaranteedBudgetRatio is relative to the maximum transmitted power and is common to all cell segments | 5GC002300-D |
| schedulWeightFactorEnabled | {FALSE; TRUE} | M | enables the proportional fair scheduling weight factor correction for EIRP control based on the power reduction factor applicable to the serving beam | 5GC002300-D |
| smoothingEffect | Enum{none, low, medium, high} | M | Determines mode on which Lyapunov control mechanism is applied (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29997) | CB013773-A |
| actEpic | Boolean | M | This parameter activates/deactivates EIRP aware POLITE Inner-loop control (EPIC). | CB013505-A |
| epicMcsThreshold | u8 (range: 0...28, step: 1, default: 5) | O | This parameter indicates the MCS threshold above which MCS reduction in EPIC is applicable. | CB013505-A |

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | L2 Variant Limitation | **First Feature** |
| zpCsiRsAssociation | u8 ENUMERATED { csiImOfCsiRsSet1, csiImOfCsiRsSet2, csiImOfCsiRsSet3, csiImOfFddNonDss, trs[CB013525-D], csiImOfFddBf8Port, csiImOfFddBf32Port [End CB013525-D] } | M | Indicate the ZP-CSI-RS’s association.   If zpCsiRsAssociation = trs: zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset shall be provided by CPRT. If zpCsiRsAssociation = csiImOfCsiRsSet1/2/3: zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset shall set to 0xFFFF by CPRT, then L2PS itself to allocate zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset, and L2PS shall return the result of zpCsiRsSlotOffset to CPRT by csiImResSlotOffset in PsCell\_CellSetupResp. This exist when actTddCsiImRm is true. If zpCsiRsAssociation = csiImOfFddNonDss:   - CPRT shall set zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset to 0xFFFF.   - L2PS shall determine the zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset (refer 5G\_L2\_16973\_replaced([11142382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23uAO_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and notify the cellZpCsiRsPeriodicity to CPRT in PsCell\_CellSetupResp. [CB013525-D] If zpCsiRsAssociation = csiImOfFddBf8Port or csiImOfFddBf32Port:   - CPRT shall set zpCsiRsPeriod and zpCsiRsSlotOffset to 0xFFFF。   - L2PS shall set zpCsiRsPeriod for csiImOfFddBf8Port as the same as cellCsiRsPeriodicity in PsCell\_CellSetupReq; zpCsiRsPeriod for csiImOfFddBf32Port as the same as cellCsiRsPeriodicityFor32Port in PsCell\_CellSetupReq.   - L2PS shall determine zpCsiRsSlotOffset (refer 5G\_L2\_16973\_replaced([11142382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23uAO_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to CPRT in PsCell\_CellSetupResp. [End CB013525-D] | [CB013525-D] L2-PS-Legacy: partially support csiImOfCsiRsSet1, csiImOfCsiRsSet2, csiImOfCsiRsSet3, csiImOfFddNonDss, trs [End CB013525-D] | CB012269-A |
| zpCsiRsPeriod | u16 [1..320], 0xFFFF | M | ZP-CSI-RS period. |  | CB012269-A |
| zpCsiRsSlotOffset | u16 [0..319], 0xFFFF | M | ZP-CSI-RS slot offset. |  | CB012269-A |
| zpCsiRsConfig | Struct zpCsiRsConfig defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_124\_replaced([10969280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ub2U_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | M | Configuration parameters of ZP-CSI-RS. |  | CB012269-A |
