**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-62.0-3**  (ID: `10969677`)

Cell Setup
crntiPoolConfig structure content:

This structure only used for FR1 cell, indicate how to split CRNTI into non overlapping part and overlapping part.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3394

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| crntiNonOverlappingPoolId[4] | u8 [0..143],0xff (invalid) |  | For FR1 TDD cell, four pool Ids if NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set to 1 with max144cells otherwise M[CB009058-A] If NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption=Max144cells  and rdCrntiAllocationOptionExtensionTdd=true [End CB009058-A] two pool Ids are valid. [CB009058-A] If NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption=Max144cells  and rdCrntiAllocationOptionExtensionTdd=false 4 pool Ids are valid [End CB009058-A] For FR1 FDD cell, only first one or first two pool Ids can be valid.; Please refer to to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more information.   Invalid pool Id shall be set as 0xff. | 5GC002546-A 5GCR-10228-A CB007737-B |
| crntiOverlappingStart | u16 | M | It seperate CRNTI whole range into two parts: non-overlapping part CRNTI < crntiOverlappingStart and overlapping part CRNTI >=crntiOverlappingStart. Used to calculate CRNTI tables during cell setup. [CB009058-A] The range of this field is 64237 - 65519 [End CB009058-A] | 5GC002546-A 5GCR-10228-A |
| crntiOverlappingPoolId | u8  [0..5],0xff | M | valid for FR1 FDD [CB009058-A] and TDD [End CB009058-A] cell, Pool Id of overlaping CRNTI, used to calculate FDD [CB009058-A] and TDD [End CB009058-A] overlapping range CRNTI list. For FDD cell, if NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set to 1 with max 144 cells, only Pool Id 0 can be set. If NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set to 0 with max 72 cells, Pool Id 0..5 can be set. [CB009058-A] For TDD cells, if NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set as Max144 and rdCrntiAllocationOptionExtensionTdd is set enabled, FR1 TDD cells are setup with 1 overlapping PoolId [End CB009058-A] 0xff is set as invalid | 5GC002546-A 5GCR-10228-A CB007737-B CB009058-A |

Cell Setup
All the parameters present in the gNB configuration (both in case of PsCell\_CellSetupReq or PsCell\_CellReconfgReq) shall be passed to the 5G-L2-PS.

The number of elements in this list indicates the number of candidate frequency resources configured for RIM-RS transmission in the network.   Note: This parameter can also provide rimRsPrbOffset list (see 5G\_UP\_5348\_replaced([11360434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucuhJfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). | CB006991-A |

| rsTransTrigger | Enum: 1: constantly trigger; 2: RI trigger 3: RS1 constantly 4: RS2 constantly | M | 'constantly trigger' means RIM-RS is configured to transmit constantly. For actNrRim equal to 'framework1, both RIM-RS Type1 and RIM-RS Type2 is configured to transmit constantly.   'RI trigger' means RIM-RS Type1 is triggered only when RI is detected. For actNrRim equal to 'framework1', RIM-RS Type2 is triggered only when RIM-RS Type1 is detected.   'RS1 constantly' means RIM-RS Type1 is configured to transmit constantly and RIM-RS Type2 is triggered only when RIM-RS Type1 is detected, when actNrRim is equal to 'framework1'.   'RS2 constantly' means RIM-RS Type2 is configured to transmit constantly and RIM-RS Type1 is triggered only when RI is detected, when actNrRim is equal to 'framework1'. | CB006991-A |

All the parameters within the rimRsConfig structure shall be filled according to the configuration received by 5G-CP-RT.

MAX\_START\_RB\_FOR\_RS is equal 4.

Parameters in rimRsConfig are common for both RIM RS1 and RIM RS2 when framework1 is configured. Only exception is rimRsTypeConfigList which contains configuration separately for RIM RS1 and RIM RS2

| rimTaThresh | 0...3846 | M | This parameter defines RIM TA threshold, meaning that all UEs with TA above TA threshold are excluded from scheduling in DL power reduced slots. 1 TA unit corresponds roughly to a distance of: - 78m for 15kHz Sub Carrier Spacing (SCS) - 39m for 30kHz Sub Carrier Spacing (SCS) | CB012719-A |
| rimMcsThresh | 0...28 | M | This parameter defines RIM MCS threshold, meaning that all UEs with MCS below this threshold are excluded from scheduling in DL power reduced slots. | CB012719-A |

Cell Setup
SlotAggregationConfig structure content

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-94.0-1**  (ID: `10970253`)

Cell Setup
SlotAggregationConfig structure content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Presence | Description | First feature |
| ulSlotAggOffTotPwrThresh | U8 | M | Threshold for exiting PUSCH Slot Aggregation mode. If the UE is currently configured for DFT-s-OFDM and the total power of the UE is greater than or equal to the value in this parameter, then the UE is configured with PUSCH transform precoding disabled (CP OFDM) and is no longer eligible for PUSCH Slot Aggregation.   It is set per NRBTS.NRCELL.ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulSlotAggOffTotPwrThresh | CB008236-A |
| ulSlotAggOnTotPwrThresh | U8 | M | Threshold for entering PUSCH Slot. If the UE is currently configured for CP OFDM and the total power of the UE is below the value in this parameter, then the UE is configured with PUSCH transform precoding enabled (DFT-s-OFDM) and is eligible for repetitions greater than 1 for PUSCH Slot Aggregation.   It is set per NRBTS.NRCELL.ulTransPrecodeCtl.ulSlotAggOnTotPwrThresh | CB008236-A |
| maxHarqBundlesUlSlotAgg | U8 | M | Maximum number of HARQ attempts for uplink PUSCH Slot Aggregation   It is set per NRBTS.NRCELL.maxHarqBundlesUlSlotAgg | CB008236-A |
| minTbsUlSlotAgg | U16 | M | This parameter sets the 5QI1 VoNR specific minimum TBS size when PUSCH Slot Aggregation is used. This is the expected TBS size for one VoNR packet assuming RoHC header compression, the use of no segmentation and including some allowance for PHRs and BSRs. Nominal values for a 13.2 Kbps or a 12.6 Kbps Vocoder is 384 bits. Nominal value for a 23.8 Kbps Vocoder is 552 bits.   It is set per NRBTS.NRCELL.minTbsUlSlotAgg | CB008236-A |
| sCellDeactInPoorRf | Enum{None=0, Deact\_Scells\_VoNr\_SAg=1 } | M | This parameter activates/deactivates disabling of all S-Cells when UE is in poor RF conditions. The value "Deact\_Scells\_VoNr\_SAg" means that SCells are deactivated when gNB enters PUSCH Slot Aggregation mode for a UE with VoNR DRB. The value "None" means no need to deactivate SCells but SCell UL scheduling will be suspended, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19252.   The modified value is taken into use for new users. The old value is applied for existing users   It is set per NRBTS.NRCELL.sCellDeactInPoorRf | CB008236-B |

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-95.0-3**  (ID: `10970279`)

Cell Setup
NbrForNonGbrBearerConfig structure content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Presence** | **Description** | **First feature** |
| **[Before CB008118-B]** CongWeightAlg **[End CB008118-B]** | Enum{0:priorityLevel 1:arpPrioPerVul} | O | This parameter congWeightAlg configures a prioritization behavior in MAC scheduling until the NBR congestion situation is resolved. There are two different algorithms possible: - 'priorityLevel': Bearers are prioritized in order of their NRDRB.priorityLevel. - 'arpPrioPerVul': First the bearers with ARP vulnerability "preemptable" are prioritized in order of the ARP priority, then the bearers with ARP vulnerability "not preemptable" also in order of ARP priority. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| **[Before CB008118-B]** congDetectPeriod **[End CB008118-B]** | U16(0-1500) | O | The parameter indicates the congestion detection period for NBR.When equal to 0 (corresponding to off), the congestion detection is disabled. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| maxNbrTrafficLimit | U8(0...90) | O | This parameter indicates the maximum percentage of radio resources that can be used for NBR traffic in uplink and downlink from the total available radio resources available for both non-GBR and GBR. It corresponds to the percentage of radio resources that are available for NBR transmissions from the PDCCH, PDSCH, and PUSCH resources. PUCCH and PRACH resources are not controlled by this parameter. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| maxPrbsPerNbrUe | U8(10...90) | M | This parameter indicates the maximum number of PRBs allocated for NBR traffic per UE in uplink and downlink. The amount of radio resources (PRBs) is calculated in % of the available PRBs depending on the system. | CB008227-A-LLF |
| nbrPdcchCongHandlingDl | Boolean | M | This parameter activates PDCCH congestion control for Downlink NBR traffic.   It is highly recommended to configure the value to 'true' if 'Nominal bitrate for non-GBR bearers' is activated, i.e. if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to 'true'. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| nbrPdcchCongHandlingUl | Boolean | M | This parameter activates PDCCH congestion control for Uplink NBR traffic. It is highly recommended to configure the value to 'true' if 'Nominal bitrate for non-GBR bearers' is activated, i.e. if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to 'true'. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| nbrPdschCongHandling | Boolean | M | This parameter activates PDSCH congestion control for NBR traffic. It is highly recommended to configure the value to 'true' if 'Nominal bitrate for non-GBR bearers' is activated, i.e. if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to 'true'. | CB008227-D-LLF |
| nbrPuschCongHandling | Boolean | M | This parameter activates PUSCH congestion control for NBR traffic. It is highly recommended to configure the value to 'true' if 'Nominal bitrate for non-GBR bearers' is activated, i.e. if actNbrForNonGbrBearers is set to 'true'. | CB008227-D-LLF |

congestionParamsConfig Structure content

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-105.0-1**  (ID: `10970421`)

Cell Setup
congestionParamsConfig Structure content :

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Presence | Description | First feature |
| congWeightAlg | Enum{0:priorityLevel 1:arpPrioPerVul} | M | This parameter congWeightAlg configures a prioritization behavior in MAC scheduling until the NBR or GBR congestion situation is resolved. There are two different algorithms possible: - 'priorityLevel': Bearers are prioritized in order of their NRDRB.priorityLevel. - 'arpPrioPerVul': First the bearers with ARP vulnerability "preemptable" are prioritized in order of the ARP priority, then the bearers with ARP vulnerability "not preemptable" also in order of ARP priority. | CB008118-B |
| congDetectPeriod | U16(100-1500) | M | The parameter indicates the congestion detection period for NBR or GBR, when the congestion detection is activated. | CB008118-B |

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-112**  (ID: `12713557`)

searchSpace

---

**2.3.2.4.0-9.0-112.0-1**  (ID: `12713558`)

Cell Setup
searchSpace Structure content

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |  |
| searchSpaceId | 0…39,[PR870031]41...50[End PR870031] | M | Identifier of the search space. [CB012631-SR-IODT-A-UPD003] for sparse search space, it is the related dense Id, common IEs also are copied from dense by CP-RT[End CB012631-SR-IODT-A-UPD003] [PR870031]Introduced 10 dummy searchSpaceId 41...50(to avoid conflict with other NIDD configured Id,max 2 Ids per BWP), it is used split search spaces when NIDD configured combined search space type (for example: 0A\_1\_2 split to 0A,1,2,the search space type1/type2 will use dummy searchSpaceId. The searchSpaceId should be unique in cell level. Combined search space is used to reduce total search space number in UE side when SSSG switching configuration(give more to dense/sparse)[End PR870031] | 5GC000742-C |  |
| associatedCoresetId | 0…11 | M | Identifier of the CORESET associated to the search space. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| monitoringSlotPeriodicity | enum {sl1, sl2, sl4, sl5, sl8, sl10, sl16, sl20, sl40, sl80, sl160, sl320, sl640, sl1280, sl2560} | M | Periodicity of the search space. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| monitoringSlotOffset | 0…2559 | M | Offset of the search space within the periodicity. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| duration | 1…2559 | M | Number of consecutive slots for which the search space exists every period as given in the monitoringSlotPeriodicity. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| monitoringSymbolsWithinSlot | u16 | M | Bitmap defining the number and position of PDCCH occasion in the slot. The most significant (left) bit represents the first OFDM in a slot. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| numberOfPdcchCandidatesInAL1 | enum {n0, n1, n2, n3, n4, n5, n6, n8} | M | number of PDCCH candidates the UE attempts to decode in AL1. For the search space defined at NIDD under BWP\_PROFILE/PDCCH/PDCCH\_CONFIG\_COMMON, the value is hardcoded by the C-Plane to “n0”. For the search space defined at NIDD under BWP\_PROFILE/PDCCH/PDCCH\_CONFIG\_DEDICATED, the value is the NIDD one. | 5GC000742-C |  |
| numberOfPdcchCandidatesInAL2 | enum {n0, n1, n2, n3, n4, n5, n6, n8} | M | Number of PDCCH candidates the UE attempts to decode in AL2. | 5GC000742-C |  |

### 2.3.2.5 Stop Scheduling

#### 2.3.2.5.0-2 Stop Scheduling Overview (ID: 10970472)

**2.3.2.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12732227`)

Stop Scheduling
Messages:

PsCell\_CellStopSchedulingReq/Resp

Purpose:

To suspend scheduling of a cell before the cell is actually released (by PsCell\_CellDeleteReq/Resp).

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_89\_replaced([11178190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeXWLfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell delete

---

#### 2.3.2.5.0-3 Stop Scheduling Description (ID: 10970478)

**2.3.2.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12732237`)

Stop Scheduling
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling in the given cell.

---

#### 2.3.2.5.0-4 Stop Scheduling Message validation (ID: 10970484)

**2.3.2.5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12732232`)

Stop Scheduling
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellStopSchedulingReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellStopSchedulingResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid, cell was identified and scheduling stopped successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_176\_replaced([10970490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjLGfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.5.0-5 Stop Scheduling Exceptions (ID: 10970490)

**2.3.2.5.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12732245`)

Stop Scheduling
Expected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-C]

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellStopSchedulingResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* nrCellGrpId IE or nrCellIdentity IE is not known or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the scheduling was not stopped successfully in the cell.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC000559-C]

Unexpected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-C]

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

[End 5GC000559-C]

[Before 5GC000559-C]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In other case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

[5GC000559-C]

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

[End 5GC000559-C]

---

### 2.3.2.6 Cell Delete

#### 2.3.2.6.0-2 Cell Delete Overview (ID: 10970520)

**2.3.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12734072`)

Cell Delete
**Messages:**

PsCell\_CellDeleteReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To delete a cell from 5G-L2-PS.

**Precondition:**

Address distribution is done.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_89\_replaced([11178190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeXWLfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell delete

---

#### 2.3.2.6.0-3 Cell Delete Description (ID: 10970526)

**2.3.2.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12734073`)

Cell Delete
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall delete the cell context and all related resources (including all the subcells).

5G-L2-PS shall also remove the related NRCELL object from PM, see 5G\_L2\_1517\_replaced([11192164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOzPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[5GC000718-N]**

Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update the nrCellList  for the cell group context, removing concerned cell.

**[End 5GC000718-N]**

**[5GC001804-A]**

For actions required for PCMD see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[End 5GC001804-A]**

**[5GC000559-C]**

If the cell context does not exist, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the procedure is successful and return a response accordingly.

**[End 5GC000559-C]**

---

#### 2.3.2.6.0-4 Cell Delete Message validation (ID: 10970532)

**2.3.2.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12734075`)

Cell Delete
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellDeleteResp message if the request message is valid, the cell was identified and deleted successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_185\_replaced([10970543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjyIvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.6.0-5 Cell Delete Concurrency handling (ID: 10970537)

**2.3.2.6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12734077`)

Cell Delete
Concurrent Cell procedures are not managed at L2-RT side and for one Cell procedure, Cells shall be handle one after the other.

If a Cell Delete procedure is initiated for one cell by 5G-CP-RT toward L2-PS, L2-LO, no other Cell procedure (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated for any other Cell until this on-going Cell Delete procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.6.0-6 Cell Delete Exceptions (ID: 10970543)

**2.3.2.6.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12734079`)

Cell Delete
**Expected Exceptions:**

**[5GC000559-C]**

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellDeleteResp message also if:

* nrCellGrpId IE or nrCellIdentity IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not deleted successfully.

**[End 5GC000559-C]**

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

**[5GC000559-C]**

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

**[End 5GC000559-C]**

---

### 2.3.2.7 System Info Configuration Request and Response

#### 2.3.2.7.0-2 System Info Configuration Request and Response Overview (ID: 10970573)

**2.3.2.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12734157`)

System Info Configuration Request and Response
**Messages:**

PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To configure Master Information Block (MIB), System Information Block type 1 (SIB1) and System Information Messages (SI-Msg).

**Precondition:**

SUBCELLGRP exists.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_238\_replaced([11194124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfohcPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): DL data on BCCH: Broadcast Control Channel transmission

---

#### 2.3.2.7.0-3 System Info Configuration Request and Response Description (ID: 10970579)

**2.3.2.7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12734158`)

System Info Configuration Request and Response
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall store the given system information configuration and start system information broadcast.

---

#### 2.3.2.7.0-4 System Info Configuration Request and Response Message validation (ID: 10970585)

**2.3.2.7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12734160`)

System Info Configuration Request and Response
Upon reception of the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the addresses and pools were configured successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_193\_replaced([10970589](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjyKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.7.0-5 System Info Configuration Request and Response Exceptions (ID: 10970589)

**2.3.2.7.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `10970601`)

System Info Configuration Request and Response
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* nrCellIdentity IE is not valid or it already exists or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not configured successfully.

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 and L2-PS failed to reallocate cell specific CSI-RS resources in time domain (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2347), L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message, set the status IE = NotOk and cause IE = NoUserPlaneResourcesAvailable.

[CB008224-A]

If the given cell identified by nrCellIdentity IE is Supplemental DL Cell FR1 (see 5G\_L2\_14855\_replaced([11141639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23puzPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall verify if:

* numberOfInformationBlocks was set to 1,
* informationBlockType was set to MasterInformationBlock
* and systemInformationIndex was set to 0.

If any of the above conditions is not satisfied, 5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message, set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause IE = InvalidParameter (see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB008224-A]

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: In addition to generic failure causes defined in 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp, there are also specific causes defined in 5G\_L3\_2597\_replaced([11022104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Q_Mv_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)) and 5G\_L3\_2600\_replaced([11022136](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Q_OP_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)).

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

#### 2.3.2.7.1 System Info Configuration Request

##### 2.3.2.7.1.0-1 System Info Configuration Request PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message content (ID: 10970613)

**2.3.2.7.1.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12745340`)

System Info Configuration Request
**PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameters** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| nrCellIdentity | 0...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity, unique across all PLMN's configured for the cell | 5GC000718-K |
| modificationPeriod | 1…65525 | M | Modification Period of System Information (unit: radio frame) | 5GC000742-A |
| numberOfInformationBlocks | 1…28 |  | Number of Information block in the message. The maximum number of SI is increased to 28 for the PWS management. | 5GC000425-A |
| >informationBlockType |  | M | Information block type. - MasterInformationBlock - SystemInformationBlock - SystemInformationMessage | 5GC000425-A 5GC000742-A |
| >systemInformationIndex | 0...m | M | Index of the Block type or SI-Msg: - 0 for the MIB - 1 for the SIB1 - or SI-Msg Index (0...n) | 5GC000742-A |
| >periodicity | 1…1024 | M | Periodicity (radio frame) of the SI-Window for a given SI (MIB, SIB1, SI-Msg) | 5GC000742-A |
| >systemInformationWindow | 1…2048 | M | Window size (number of slots) where the UE is able to find PDCCH/PDSCH resources used for the SI transmissions. | 5GC000742-A 5GC000742-B |
| >modificationTimeFrame | (0): mibOrSiWindow or (1): modificationPeriod | M | Time frame to start the transmission of the new SI | 5GC000742-A |
| >pwsType | u8: [0-7] | O | This field is present only if the Information block type is set to SystemInformationBlock or SystemInformationMessage. Bitmap indicating the presence or not of PWS data in the SIB1 and SI-Msg: - b0: Earthquake and Tsunami Warning System        (ETWS) primary notification. - b1: Earthquake and Tsunami Warning System        (ETWS) secondary notification. - b2: Commercial Mobile Alert System (CMAS)        notification. | 5GC000746-A |
| >pwsSibBitOffset | u16: [0-2942] | O | This field is present only when the Information block type is set to SystemInformationMessage. It is the start position of the PWS SIB in the encodedL3MsgPayload of the SI-Msg. | 5GC000746-A |
| >encodedL3MsgLength |  | M | Encoded BCCH-BCH or BCCH-DL-SCH Message length with padding bits | 5GC000425-A 5GC000521-B |
| >encodedL3MsgPayload |  | M | Byte aligned encoded BCCH-BCH or BCCH-DL-SCH Message payload with padding bits | 5GC000425-A |
| >sfnOffset |  | O | Position in bits of the field systemFrameNumber in BCCH-BCH-Message: Master Information Block. This field corresponds to 6 MSB Bit of the System Frame Number (SFN). This field is present only if the Information block type is set to "MasterInformationBlock". | 5GC000425-A |
| >sfnLength |  | O | Length in bits of the field systemFrameNumber in BCCH-BCH-Message: Master Information Block corresponds to the MSB Bit of the System Frame Number (SFN). This field is present only if the Information block type is set to "MasterInformationBlock". | 5GC000425-A |
| >hyperSfnOffset |  | O | Position(from MSB) in bits of the field hyperSFN-r17 in SIB1 PDU, hyperSFN-r17 is fixed 10bits length encoded in SIB1 payload by CP-RT, from high to lower bit. 5G-L2-PS use it to fill  hyperSFN-r17 in SIB1 when broadcast SIB1.Refer to 5G\_L2\_18984\_replaced([11142585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23vOXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | CB012544-B |
| >pcchConfig | structure, refered to 5G\_L2\_IF\_197\_replaced([10970659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UkZNPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | O | PCCH config parameters Note: It is optionally available if informationBlockType is set to SystemInformationBlock (i.e. SIB1) This field is present only when the following conditions are met: - The "InformationBlockType" is set to   "SystemInformationBlock". - The "pwsType" is set to 0. - The PCCH configuration is modified (cell setup and   online modification of the PCCH parameters). | 5GC000733-H |
| >maxNumOfPagingRecords | 1 … 32 | O | Indicates maximal number of paging records for paging message.   Parameter is present only in cell setup and later if its value is modified. Valid only for FR1. Defined in NRBTS/NRCELL/maxNumPagingRecords. | CB010774-A |
| needReturnCsirs | Boolean | M | Indicates whether new cell specific CSI-RS resource allocation is expected:  - FALSE: new cell specific CSI-RS resource allocation is not expected by client, L2-PS needs to response NOK in case of elderly allocated CSI-RS resource overlaps with Paging / OSI slots newly evaluated. - TRUE: new cell specific CSI-RS resource allocation is expected by client, L2-PS needs to response the newly evaluated CSI-RS resource in case of elderly allocated CSI-RS resource overlaps with Paging / OSI slots newly evaluated or the elderly allocated CSI-RS resource otherwise. If PsCell\_CellSetupReq::dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 and PsCell\_CellSetupReq::cellWithSib1 is set to TRUE **and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, needReturnCsirs must be set to TRUE within the 1st PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message by client (i.e.CPRT).**  If actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is true **or actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true** , needReturnCsirs must be set to false.\*\*\*\* | 01840533 |
| [CB014330-D] pagingTargetRateIndex [End CB014330-D] | Integer (0..30), Step size 1 | O | Target rate index of PDSCH for paging: If NRBTS.NRCELL.pagingTargetRate is configured, Parameter is mandatorily present during cell setup procedure, and later it is present only when its value is modified or dciPagingAggregationLevel is modified with pagingTargetRateIndex is 0, else parameter is not present.  0: target rate is associated to the Aggregation Level selected for paging  1...30: target rate is as specified Configured by NIDD parameter NRBTS.NRCELL.pagingTargetRate | CB014330-D |

##### 2.3.2.7.1.0-2 System Info Configuration Request IE Definitions (ID: 12734152)

**2.3.2.7.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10970659`)

System Info Configuration Request
**pcchConfig**

---

**2.3.2.7.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12734156`)

System Info Configuration Request
**pcchConfig structure content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| defaultPagingCycle | ENUMERATED {rf32. rf64, rf128, rf256} | M | Default paging cycle value | 5GC000733-H |
| n | ENUMERATED {oneT, halfT, quarterT, oneEighthT, oneSixteenthT} | M | number of total paging frames in a paging cycle | 5GC000733-H |
| pfOffset | 0...15 | M | offset used for paging frame determination; chosen values are one to one corresponding to chosen values of n | 5GC000733-H |
| ns | ENUMERATED {four, two, one} | M | number of paging occassions for a paging frame | 5GC000733-H |
| firstPdcchMonitoringOccasionOfPo[ns] | 0...17919 | M | first PDCCH monitoring occasion of each paging occasion for the paging frame   **[5GC000733-G] The parameter is optional. If its value is 65535, 5G-L2-PS shall consider that the parameter is not configured by operator.**   The size of the parameter is the number of paging occasion per paging frame i.e. ns. **[Before 5GC000733-I] The range of entries for the parameter is based on combination of subcarrier spacing and the number of total paging frames in a paging cycle n.** **[5GC000733-I] Value range for each entry is 0...K-1, where K is the number of PDCCH monitoring occasions in paging search space from start of the paging frame and before start of next paging frame.**   **[Before 5GC000733-I] NOTE: The value provided in NIDD is OFDM symbol index within one radio frame. At User Plane it will get** slot index within a radio frame = floor(firstPDCCH-MonitoringOccasionOfPO/14). **[5GC000733-I] Each entry in the parameter indicates a PDCCH monitoring occassion in paging search space for the paging frame. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3918 for details of numbering of PDCCH monitoring occasions.** | 5GC000733-H |

### 2.3.2.8 Public Warnig System Requests, Response and Indication

#### 2.3.2.8.0-2 Public Warnig System Requests, Response and Indication Overview (ID: 10970726)

**2.3.2.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12734167`)

Public Warnig System Requests, Response and Indication
**Messages:**

PsCell\_PwsMsgAddReq/Resp

PsCell\_PwsMsgDelReq/Resp

PsCell\_PwsMsgReplaceReq/Resp

PsCell\_PwsMsgReportInd

**Purpose:**

To manage the active PWS messages list, the 5G-L2-PS has to broadcast in a System Information message (SI-Msg) handling PWS System Information Block.

To report the information about PWS message broadcast conditions.

**Precondition:**

SUBCELLGRP exists.

**Addressing:**

The requests are sent to the PsCell address.

The responses and report are sent to the address where the requests was sent from.

**Description:**

Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall add, delete or replace the PWS message in the PWS active message list.

When the PWS message is removed from the active message list or when the PWS channel overload is detected, the 5G-L2-PS shall report the information to the Cell layer.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_RAN\_UP\_TBD: DL data on BCCH: Public Warning System management

**Expected Exceptions:**

If the 5G-L2-PS is not able to process the PsCell\_PwsMsgAdd/Del/ReplaceReq messages, the negative acknowledgement is sent in the PsCell\_PwsMsgAdd/Del/ReplaceResp with a status set to EStatus5G\_NotOk, a specific cause and diagnostic information.

Not applicable for the PsCell\_PwsMsgReportInd message.

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

None.

---

#### 2.3.2.8.1 Public Warning System Message Add Request and Response

##### 2.3.2.8.1.1 Public Warning System Message Add Request

###### 2.3.2.8.1.1.0-1 Public Warning System Message Add Request PsCell_PwsMsgAddReq (ID: 10970744)

**2.3.2.8.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12734169`)

Public Warning System Message Add Request
**PsCell\_PwsMsgAddReq message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | 5GC000746-A |
| pwsMsgId | u8: [0...31] | M | Internal PWS message identifier between the C-Plane and the U-Plane. | 5GC000746-A |
| pwsNotificationType | enum{cmas, primaryEtws, secondaryEtws} | M | Indicate the type of notification to broadcast. | 5GC000746-A |
| repetitionPeriod | u32: [0…217 – 1] | M | Time interval (seconds) between 2 consecutive broadcasts of the PWS notification. | 5GC000746-A |
| nbOfBroadcastReq | u16: [0…65535] | M | Expected broadcasts of the PWS message. | 5GC000746-A |
| nbOfPwsSibSegment | u8: [0...31] | M | Number of PWS SIB segments available in the payload. | 5GC000746-A |
| pwsSibSegmentSize | u16: [0-2976] | M | Size (bit) of a PWS SIB segment in the payload. | 5GC000746-A |

##### 2.3.2.8.1.2 Public Warning System Message Add Response

###### 2.3.2.8.1.2.0-1 Public Warning System Message Add Response PsCell_PwsMsgAddResp (ID: 10970756)

**2.3.2.8.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `10970768`)

Public Warning System Message Add Response
PsCell\_PwsMsgAddResp message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | 5GC000746-A |
| messageResult | Structure | M |  | 5GC000746-A |

### 2.3.2.9 Cell Reconfiguration

#### 2.3.2.9.0-2 Cell Reconfiguration Overview (ID: 10970923)

**2.3.2.9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12734336`)

Cell Reconfiguration
**Messages:**

PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To Reconfigure a cell from 5G-L2-PS.

**Precondition:**

Cell exists.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_100\_replaced([11178581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeZLUvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT cell Reconfiguration

---

#### 2.3.2.9.0-3 Cell Reconfiguration Description (ID: 10970929)

**2.3.2.9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12734338`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update the cell context for the on line modifiable parameters contained in the message and all related resources. The new values shall be valid for all (existing and new) UEs in the cell.

---

#### 2.3.2.9.0-4 Cell Reconfiguration Message validation (ID: 10970934)

**2.3.2.9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12734339`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the cell was reconfigured successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1814\_replaced([10970947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UmOYfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.9.0-5 Cell Reconfiguration Concurrency handling (ID: 10970940)

**2.3.2.9.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12734340`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Concurrent Cell procedures are not managed at L2-RT side and for one Cell procedure, Cells shall be handle one after the other.

If a Cell Reconfiguration procedure is initiated for one cell by 5G-CP-RT toward L2-PS, L2-LO, no other Cell procedure (Setup, Delete or Reconfiguration) shall be concurrently initiated for any other Cell until this on-going Cell Reconfiguration procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.9.0-6 Cell Reconfiguration Exceptions (ID: 10970947)

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `10970952`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Generic handling

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-1.0-11**  (ID: `12698185`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Expected Exceptions:  
  
Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Let's define set of resource group checks as (S1):  
•    if there is at least one resource group or default resource group with id out of range configured in resource group configuration,  
•    if there is more than one configuration for resource group or default resource group in resource group configuration,  
•    if minQuota within any resource group is out of range [0..100],  
•    if maxQuota within any resource group is out of range [1..100],  
•    if there is at least one resource group where minQuota > maxQuota,  
•    if sum of minQuotas in all resource groups is greater than 100,  
•    if there is at least one default resource group using unconfigured resource group,  
•    if there is at least one bearer configured with default resource group which was not configured in resource group configuration,

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value in following cases:  
    1.    nrCellGrpId IE or nrCellIdentity IE is not known  
    2.    The request message is not valid  
    3.    The resources were not reconfigured successfully  
    4.    At least one of the following rules is fulfilled:  
        4.1.     actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to pusch, pucchPusch, puschSrs or pucchPuschSrs but clpcPusch is missing in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
        4.2.    actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to pucch, pucchPusch or pucchPuschSrs but clpcPucch is missing in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
    5.    sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true and:  
        5.1.    dlResourceGroupConfig is not present. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
        5.2.    (S1) checks are performed for resource groups in dlResourceGroupConfig. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
    6.    ulResourceGroupConfig is present, then (S1) checks are performed for resource groups in ulResourceGroupConfig. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
    7.  [Before CB010315-A]  actNrRim is set to value other than "disabled" in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq while any element of Cell Setup configuration ulSubcellList contains eCpriFlag = False. Set the cause IE = InvalidParameter  
    8. [End CB010315-A]   actEirpControl is equal to True and was memorized at True in L2-PS BD in previous state ([11118723](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqFAifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). Set the cause IE = Undefined  
For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
  
In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were reconfigured by the 5G-L2-PS.  
  
For exceptions related to Supplemental DL Cell FR1, see: 5G\_L2\_16606\_replaced([11163082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25kaUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
  
If ssBlockPower received in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq:powerChannelReconfiguration (5G\_L2\_IF\_6060\_replaced([10971679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Up4wPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is out of range, L2PS shall set the default value of MIN (-903) or MAX (0) depending on whether the received value out of the range is closer to MAX or MIN.

Unexpected Exceptions:  
In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Note:  
Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10971016`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Artificial-load-specific

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10971021`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Invalid patternId exception

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10971028`)

Cell Reconfiguration
For Invalid patternId exception, see: 5G\_L2\_IF\_6296\_replaced([10967142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2USsavu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10971033`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Invalid energySavingState exception

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10971039`)

Cell Reconfiguration
When the request message is received and the patternIdsForArtificialLoadForEmfTestMode list from structure artificialLoadInfo (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_111\_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is NOT empty and emfTotalTargetLoad is greater than 0, 5G-L2-PS shall access information about the energySavingState of the given cell from the latest PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2737\_replaced([10973702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U2tHfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq was received and the energySavingState IE was set to reducedEnergySaving, 5G-L2-PS shall respond with status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause = InvalidParameter (see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Rationale: The cell shall not be in reducedEnergySaving state when DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation is enabled.

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12977723`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Power Saving

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12977724`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Expected Exceptions for Power Saving:

[PR867026] For TDD and FDD: [End PR867026]

1. [Before PR867026] If actNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving = TRUE in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq and requirements for online activation of power saving are not met ([12763413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m61BxIPzEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), then  5G-L2-PS shall respond PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp to 5G-CP-RT with status EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause InvalidParameter and cell does not go into power saving state. [End PR867026]

[PR867026] If actNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving is changed to TRUE in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq , then 5G-L2-PS shall log warning print because requirements for online activation of power saving are not met ([12763413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m61BxIPzEfCOGMMH109ICw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showArtifactPage&artifactURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FMD_XF2DofvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ&oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9&artifactInModule=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fresources%2FBI_m61BxIPzEfCOGMMH109ICw&componentURI=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Frm-projects%2F_44AJ0J5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA%2Fcomponents%2F_5J4kAJ5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA"))  during PsCell\_CellSetupReq and return status IE: EStatus5G\_Ok.  [End PR867026]

1. If actEirpControl=FALSE and actNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving=FALSE in PsCell\_CellSetupReq and both are changed to TRUE in the same PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq, then 5G-L2-PS shall log info print, skip potential validation of:
2. eirpControlConfigExt.dftBeamResponseNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving AND
3. eirpControlForSrsDftBeam

and return a PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp message with status IE: EStatus5G\_Ok.

This is because both dftBeamResponseNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving and eirpControlForSrsDftBeam can be sent after PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message, in PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message, when IE actEirpControl is reconfigured to TRUE.

1. If actNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving is changed to TRUE in PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq again (TRUE -> FALSE -> TRUE)  and state of energySavingState = reducedEnergySaving in PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq, then 5G-L2-PS shall log warning print because state is not cleared during PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq.

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `12982576`)

Cell Reconfiguration
SSSG parameter reconfigration

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12982578`)

Cell Reconfiguration
[Before PR867429]Expected Exceptions for SSSG reconfiguration:

if PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq has actSssgSwitching reconfigured to True or reconfigure parameters for sparseSSGroupListPerBwp, L2-PS applied accept new parameter as valid  when there is no any UE working in previous sparse SSSG, or else L2-PS pending sends response, untill all UEs are switched to dense or max waiting timer expires(note that, the UE which is not finished maybe dropped due to sparse PDCCH mismactch in gNB side. But suppose L2-PS has reserved enough time to switching all UEs).[End PR867429]

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-5**  (ID: `13395213`)

Cell Reconfiguration
PDCCH specific

---

**2.3.2.9.0-6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13395214`)

Cell Reconfiguration
Upon receiving a PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall validate the dciDedicatedAggregationLevel parameter.

If all the following conditions are met

1)In a [Before CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]K2 slot([11114685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
possible K2 slot [End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001],  If any of the configured Bandwidth Parts (BWP) other than initial BWP in cell reconfiguration has  dciDedicatedAggregationLevel  configured and provides only a single PDCCH occasion from all its UE-Specific Search Spaces (SS) combined.

2)The CORESET size corresponding to that single PDCCH occasion is smaller than 2 \* dciDedicatedAggregationLevel.

5G-L2-PS shall send a response message PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp with   
the status IE set to NOK (EStatus5G\_NotOk) and   
the cause IE set to InvalidParameter (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter) and  
[CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
the needForRollback IEshall be set to false and    
[End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
a detailed diagnostic information for this failure as defined in [13359340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7tLkp_H3EfC0Z6kKit-MzQ).

Note:

[Before CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
K2 slots are identified based on the existing availableDlSlotsBitMapForK2Resources calculated upon cell setup request.  
[CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]  
The possible K2 slots are determined as follows:

* For TDD frame structures(1208, 1116, 1070) for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is supported, all DL/special slots that precede the next UL slot by up to k2rimMax ([13432384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aDWAAx7VEfG-foklaHnAaA)).
* For TDD frame structures for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is not supported DL/Special slots that are rrmK2min slots ahead of UL slots ([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
* For FDD, all DL slots shall be considered as K2 slots even in a DSS cell.

[End CB014330-SR-H-UPD001]

Validation of dciDedicatedAggregationLevel  parameter shall be done after existing validations of cell reconfiguration request are completed, to prioritize the critical faults

---

#### 2.3.2.9.0-8 Cell Reconfiguration PsCell_CellReconfigurationResp Message Content (ID: 10971278)

**2.3.2.9.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `10971290`)

Cell Reconfiguration
**PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| messageResult | NA (structure) | M |  | 5GC000718-C |
| >status | EStatus5G\_Ok EStatus5G\_NotOk | M |  | 5GC000718-C |
| >cause | u32 ECause5G\_ | M | See available  values in 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | 5GC000718-C |
| needForRollback | TRUE, FALSE | M | If status IE is set to “NotOk” and if needForRollback IE is set to “TRUE”, the server indicates to the client that in case of failure internal clean-up is not complete and the state of the context is not stable. The server expects context clean-up actions from the client. | 5GC000559-B |
| nrCellGrpId | 0...3071 | M | See 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | 5GC000718-C |
| nrCellIdentity | 0...2^36-1 | M |  | 5GC000718-C 5GC000718-K |
| **[CNI-106397] diagnosticInformation** **[End CNI-106397]** | array[14] of u32 | M | diagnosticInformationInformation used by the C-Plane to raise an alarm. | CNI-106397 |

Only needed when cell is a subject for massive MIMO muting for energy efficiency (see 5G\_L3\_15819\_replaced([11022741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Upnf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))).* | CB008133-B |
| normalizedBeamGain[] | uint16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | O | For each beam, normalized beam gain per cell segment shall be provided in Q1.15 linear scale. 1 value corresponds to maxBeamGain numberOfBeams is unchanged from cellSetup and configured according to bfSetup>numberOfBeams   The list size: – minimum is 1, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT where:   MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM = 64, MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT = 60   In case of TDD [CB009543-C1] or FDD [End CB009543-C1] supercell (NRCELL.actSupercell = true), The list size: – minimum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM*2, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell     CP-RT fills the first "numberOfBeamsInSupercell \* numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell " number of elements of the list with valid values. Rest of the elements are filled with 0.   where,   MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM = 64,   numberOfBeamsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells,   numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells | 5GC002300-B |
| normalizedBeamGainForNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving[] | uint16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_BEAM\*MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | O | Additional *normalizedBeamGain values for reducedEnergySaving mode. Only needed when cell is a subject for massive MIMO muting for energy efficiency (see 5G\_L3\_15819\_replaced([11022741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_Upnf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))).* | CB008133-B |
| powerReductionFactor[] | int16 [1…MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT] | O | power reduction factor to determine maximum normalized EIRP over timeAveragingWindow Allowed range of values is -25...0 [dB] per 0.1 [dB] step Note: int16 value must be divided by 10 to obtain a step of 0.1 The list size: – minimum is 1, – maximum is MAX\_NUM\_OF\_CELL\_SEGMENT = 60   In case of TDD [CB009543-C1] or FDD [End CB009543-C1] supercell (NRCELL.actSupercell = true) The list size: – minimum is 2, – maximum is numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell   CP-RT fills the first "numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell" number of elements of the list with valid values.   where, numberOfCellSegmentsInSupercell = NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells | 5GC002300-B |
| eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow | 1..30 minutes | O | Sliding window size for EIRP control   The step of the sliding window is defined by eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize   A maximum of 3600 samples per window is supported (for example 6 minutes with 100ms sampling period or 30 minutes with 500ms sampling period) | 5GC002300-B |
| eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize | 100..1000 ms per 20ms step | O | Sampling period for EIRP measurements and EIRP control sliding window step size   eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize must divide eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow   eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize is only expected at feature activation and shall not be modified while feature is active | 5GC002300-C |
| minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode | Enum {actualEirpBudgetRatio, maxPowerBudgetRatio} | O | defines the mode applicable for the minimum guaranteed budget ratio of EIRP control | 5GC002300-D |
| minGuaranteedBudgetRatio | 0..1 per 0.01 step | O | defines the minimum guaranteed budget that shall be available in any EIRP control window step size.   If minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode is configured to actualEirpBudgetRatio then minGuaranteedBudgetRatio is relative to the power reduction factor of each cell segment.   If minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode is configured to maxPowerBudgetRatio then minGuaranteedBudgetRatio is relative to the maximum transmitted power and is common to all cell segments | 5GC002300-D |
| schedulWeightFactorEnabled | {FALSE; TRUE} | O | enables the proportional fair scheduling weight factor correction for EIRP control based on the power reduction factor applicable to the serving beam | 5GC002300-D |
| smoothingEffect | Enum{none, low, medium, high} | M | Determines mode on which Lyapunov control mechanism is applied (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29997) | CB013773-A |
| actEpic | Boolean | O | This parameter activates/deactivates EIRP aware POLITE Inner-loop control (EPIC). | CB013505-A |
| epicMcsThreshold | u8 (range: 0...28, step: 1, default: 5) | O | This parameter indicates the MCS threshold above which MCS reduction in EPIC is applicable. | CB013505-A |

The structure is defined if actEirpControl is set to TRUE.

**2.3.2.9.0-9.0-14**  (ID: `10971659`)

Cell Reconfiguration
**wbSbSwitchOnlineConfig - OBSOLETED**

---

**2.3.2.9.0-9.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `13395732`)

Cell Reconfiguration
5G-CP-RT shall sends CpRtCm\_ShutdownResp back to M-Plane.

CpRtCm\_ShutdownResp.cellsFailedToShutdownList contains all nrCellIdentity of the cell that failed to shutdown due to any exception as listed below.

Note: After 5G-CP-RT informs O&M about the outcome of the graceful shutdown,  5G-CP-RT will receive CpRtCm\_CellConfigUpdateReq from O&M that contains CellToDeleteList [5G\_L3\_FLOW\_77111\_replaced([11000012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_77h6Wfu9Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))] or CellToDeactivateList [5G\_L3\_FLOW\_77946\_replaced([11000469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_77k9ofu9Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

**[CB008521-A] *Note 2: All internal 5G-CP-RT tasks that change 5G-CP-RT configuration data and are triggered by CpRtCm\_ShutdownReq must be finished before sending this message to keep data consistency needed in the High Availability [5G\_L3\_15481\_replaced([11069320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BDPgTP_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))]. \*\*[End CB008521-A]***\*\*

### 2.3.2.10 Cell Post Reconfiguration

#### 2.3.2.10.0-2 Cell Post Reconfiguration Overview (ID: 12583503)

**2.3.2.10.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12575681`)

Cell Post Reconfiguration
**Messages:**

PsCell\_CellPostReconfigurationReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To switch the semiDynamicBW cell mode between nominal mode and limited mode.

**Precondition:**

the cell exists.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:  
to be defined**

---

#### 2.3.2.10.0-3 Cell Post Reconfiguration Description (ID: 12583530)

**2.3.2.10.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12575685`)

Cell Post Reconfiguration
Description:

Upon reception of the request, if the parameter semiDynamicBWSize is present and valid, 5G-L2-Ps shall update CSI-RS reference signals setting to the number of PRBs of the bandwidth of the cell in limited bandwidth mode.

---

#### 2.3.2.10.0-4 Cell Post Reconfiguration Message validation (ID: 12583536)

**2.3.2.10.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12575686`)

Cell Post Reconfiguration
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellReconfigurationResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the cell was reconfigured successfully.

if the message is received and the IE semiDynamicBwSize is absent, 5G-L2-PS shall return a status OK, the IE is ignored and the feature is not impacted.   
reason: future use of the message cellPostReconfReq.

For exception handling, refer to below artifact

---

#### 2.3.2.10.0-5 Cell Post Reconfiguration Exceptions (ID: 12583542)

**2.3.2.10.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12575689`)

Cell Post Reconfiguration
Expected Exceptions:

1) If the cell is configured as a semiDynamicBW cell, corresponding to bandwith =40Mhz and smallBWP=20Mhz and small BWP is not aligned with the bottom of the large BWP, and no prb blanking,

there is an exception if the value of semiDynamicBWSize is out of range, 5G-L2-PS shall return a response with the status notOk.

2) If nrCellIdentity is not known, 5G-L2-PS shall return a response with the status notOk

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

---

#### 2.3.2.10.0-6 Cell Post Reconfiguration PsCell_CellPostReconfigurationReq message (ID: 12575602)

**2.3.2.10.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12575335`)

Cell Post Reconfiguration
PsCell\_CellPostReconfigurationReq message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| nrCellGrpId | 0...3071 | M | See 5G\_UP\_2720\_replaced([11391897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufbP1fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | CB012299-B |
| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | CB012299-B |
| semiDynamicBwSize | Enum{  0: nominalBandwidth,  1: limitedBandwidth,  } | O | This parameter allows switching between nominal and limited bandwidth mode Refer to the artifact [12524086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fCp_8BoZEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) | CB012299-B |

---

### 2.3.2.11 Graceful Cell Shutdown

#### 2.3.2.11.0-2 Graceful Cell Shutdown Overview (ID: 10971739)

**2.3.2.11.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12734549`)

Graceful Cell Shutdown
Messages:

PsCell\_DlCellShutdownReq/Resp

Purpose:

To reduce the DL power of SSb by 3 dB at each power reduction step:

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_97\_replaced([11178444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeYkRvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): L2-RT Graceful Cell Shutdown

---

#### 2.3.2.11.0-3 Graceful Cell Shutdown Description (ID: 10971743)

**2.3.2.11.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12734552`)

Graceful Cell Shutdown
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall reduce the DL power of SSb by 3 dB at each power reduction step by increasing pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB value. (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2584)

If nrCellIdentity are known, 5G-L2-PS shall return a response with OK status after shutdownWindow + 10s.

(5G\_L2\_IF\_240\_replaced([10971755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Up4zfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 2.3.2.11.0-4 Graceful Cell Shutdown Exceptions (ID: 10971749)

**2.3.2.11.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12734554`)

Graceful Cell Shutdown
Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

If nrCellIdentity are not known, 5G-L2-PS shall return a response with NOK status immediately after reception of PsCell\_DlShutDownReq.

In other case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

---

#### 2.3.2.11.0-5 Graceful Cell Shutdown PsCell_DlCellShutdownReq (ID: 10971755)

**2.3.2.11.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12734556`)

Graceful Cell Shutdown
PsCell\_DlCellShutdownReq message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | 5GC000501-A |
| shutdownStepAmount | 1….16 | M | The shutdown step amount for stepwise output power reduction | 5GC000501-A |
| shutdownWindow | 6, 12, 18..., 180 | M | Duration of the whole cell shutdown operation for one Power Reduction operation | 5GC000501-A |

---

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M |  | 5GC000501-A 5GC000501-B |

### 2.3.2.12 Dss Cell Create CRM Client

#### 2.3.2.12.0-2 Dss Cell Create CRM Client Overview (ID: 10971779)

**2.3.2.12.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12741977`)

Dss Cell Create CRM Client
Messages:

PsCell\_DssCellCreateCrmClientReq/Resp

Purpose:

To exchange information related to Xp header and 5G-L2-PS EQID address.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_12693

---

#### 2.3.2.12.0-3 Dss Cell Create CRM Client Description (ID: 10971784)

**2.3.2.12.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12741978`)

Dss Cell Create CRM Client
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall

* store the DL PS XpIf Routing Header for use when sending messages to CRM.
* store the address of the client (as destination address for indication messages)

5G-L2-PS shall respond with own EQID address used for communication with XpIf, see 5G\_L2\_2842\_replaced([11140255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23iaBfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**2.3.2.12.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12741980`)

Dss Cell Create CRM Client
Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

None

---

### 2.3.2.14 Dss Crm Keep Alive

Dss Crm Keep Alive
Messages:

PsCell\_DssCellCrmKeepAliveReq/Resp

Purpose:

To start/stop keep alive procedure between CRM client and CRM

Precondition:

Cell exists, Dss Cell Xp If Address completed.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

**2.3.2.14.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12746926`)

Dss Crm Keep Alive
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall start (true) / stop (false) the keep alive procedure.

Response does not carry any specific information.

Dss Cell Crm Protocol Version
Messages:

### 2.3.2.16 Dss Cell Set Mute State

#### 2.3.2.16.0-2 Dss Cell Set Mute State Overview (ID: 10971964)

**2.3.2.16.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12765016`)

Dss Cell Set Mute State
Messages:

PsCell\_DssCellSetMuteStateReq/Resp

Purpose:

To inform 5G-L2-PS about keeping the cell silent.

Precondition:

Cell exists, to unmute, a resource allocation should have been received before. Typically, this is the initial resource allocation received by DssCellCrmClientCfg procedure.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_12713

---

#### 2.3.2.16.0-3 Dss Cell Set Mute State Description (ID: 10971970)

**2.3.2.16.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12765017`)

Dss Cell Set Mute State
On receipt of the message, the cell is muted (no scheduling and SSB is powered down) or unmuted.

Response does not carry any specific information.

### 2.3.2.19 Dss Cell Crm Allocation

#### 2.3.2.19.0-2 Dss Cell Crm Allocation Overview (ID: 10972183)

**2.3.2.19.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12772182`)

Dss Cell Crm Allocation
Messages:

PsCell\_DssCellCrmAllocInd/Ack

Purpose:

To inform CP-RT about reception of EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST, indicating that NR cell and LTE partner cell match.

The ack is sent to the address where the indication was sent from.

### 2.3.2.20 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication

#### 2.3.2.20.0-2 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication Overview (ID: 10972225)

**2.3.2.20.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13327674`)

Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication
**Messages:**

PsCell\_PowerSavingLoadMeasurementInd

**Purpose:**

Report to C-Plane the cell load measurement for energy saving management by:

* cell switch-off**,**
* load-based MIMO muting for Energy Efficiency
* [CB014095-B] online [End CB014095-B] massive MIMO muting FR1 for energy efficiency

**Precondition:**

Cell exists.

**Addressing:**

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

[CB014095-B] [12770633:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Z6kEi4iVEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) Online Activate Cell Load Measurement for mMIMO TX Power Saving [End CB014095-B]

---

#### 2.3.2.20.0-3 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication Description (ID: 10972248)

**2.3.2.20.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `10972266`)

Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication
5G-L2-PS send Power Saving Load Measurement indication message, that give to C-Plane the cell load for energy saving management by:

* cell switch-off,
* load-based MIMO muting for Energy Efficiency,
* [CB008133-A]massive MIMO muting FR1 for energy efficiency[End CB008133-A]

See [5G\_L2\_IF\_306\_replaced([10972282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UtjK_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

This message is transmitted periodically, only if:

* the load-based power saving activation flag (actNrLBPowerSaving) received from CP-RT within PsCell\_CellSetupReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or from latest PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq  (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , is TRUE.
* or the load-based MIMO muting for Energy Efficiency feature activation flag (actNrLBRTXPowerSaving) received from CP-RT within PsCell\_CellSetupReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or from the latest PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is TRUE,
* [CB008133-A]or the "Massive MIMO muting FR1 for energy efficiency" feature is active (actNrLBmMimoRTXPowerSaving = True (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))))[End CB008133-A].

NOTE: Upon reception of the Cell setup Request [5G\_L2\_IF\_49\_replaced([10966848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQ3OPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))], 5G-L2-PS shall store the address of the client (as destination address for Power Saving Load Measurement indication messages).

---

#### 2.3.2.20.0-4 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication Message periodicity (ID: 10972271)

**2.3.2.20.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12772241`)

Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication
This message is transmitted periodically, the period is determined by an R&D parameter R&D parameter *rdLoadPowerSavingAvgConst  []*

---

#### 2.3.2.20.0-5 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication Exceptions (ID: 10972276)

**2.3.2.20.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12772242`)

Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication
Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

None

---

#### 2.3.2.20.0-6 Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication PsCell_PowerSavingLoadMeasurementInd (ID: 10972282)

**2.3.2.20.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10972293`)

Cell Power Saving Load Measurement indication

### 2.3.2.21 Beam Configuration update

#### 2.3.2.21.0-2 Beam Configuration update Overview (ID: 12535982)

**2.3.2.21.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12655667`)

Beam Configuration update
Messages:

PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq/Resp

PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq/Resp see [10972300: Cell PMI Beam Data Set](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UtjLvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Purpose:

To support BF Cell's beam parameter:

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.tiltOffset

[CB014301-A]

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.lowerEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.upperEdgeAngle

[End CB014301-A]

[CB014301-B]

basicBeamSet

[End CB014301-B]

online change.

Precondition:

Cell is setup and is beamforming enabled.

Addressing:

The request is sent from CPRT to PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

[12538884: Beam Configuration Update](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8eFycSAoEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

#### 2.3.2.21.0-3 Beam Configuration update Description (ID: 12536010)

**2.3.2.21.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12655679`)

Beam Configuration update
When BF Cell's beam parameter:

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.tiltOffset

[CB014301-A]

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.lowerEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.upperEdgeAngle

[End CB014301-A]

is online changed, many beam forming related parameters and vectors need to be updated from CPRT to L2PS. The updated is done via beam configuration update procedure but not cell reconfiguration procedure for bellow reason:

1. The beamforming related parameters and vectors makes large message size, so it shall be avoided to add the parameters to a already large message like PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq;
2. If the online change is failed, it is hard to roll back across all modules (L2PS, 5G-CP-RT, L1, RF) as other single parameter reconfiguration, so make a new procedure to keep the cell reconfiguration procedure and beam configuration update procedure not impacted by each other;
3. To reuse PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq(see [10972376: PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuKS_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) mostly, PMI beam's information (included in PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq) impacted by changed:

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.tiltOffset

[CB014301-A]

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.lowerEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.upperEdgeAngle

[End CB014301-A]

is updated as [10972300: Cell PMI Beam Data Set](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UtjLvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ).

---

#### 2.3.2.21.0-4 Beam Configuration update Message validation (ID: 12536223)

**2.3.2.21.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12536224`)

Beam Configuration update
Upon reception of the PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateResp message and set the messageResult->status = EStatus5G\_Ok and messageResult->cause=2 if the request message is valid.

For more exception handling, see [12536232: Exceptions](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KhocMR9ZEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

#### 2.3.2.21.0-5 Beam Configuration update Concurrency handling (ID: 12536536)

**2.3.2.21.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12536537`)

Beam Configuration update
Concurrent beam configuration update procedures are not managed at L2-RT side.

There is no message concurrency in the procedure.

---

#### 2.3.2.21.0-6 Beam Configuration update Exceptions (ID: 12536232)

**2.3.2.21.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `13363152`)

Beam Configuration update
When receiving the PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq:

* if the cell is not BF [Before CB008577-E]TDD[End CB008577-E] FR1,  the message is not valid, L2-PS shall send  PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateResp message and set the status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause=2 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter).

For any other parameter not valid or not in line with the interface description in [12536044: PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vGqq8B9PEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), also can send PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateResp message and set the status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause=2 (ECause5G\_InvalidParameter) as in [11375790: Response Message Status and Cause](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

When receiving the PsCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq with BeamReconfigDeployment.leftEdgeAngle, rightEdgeAngle, upperEdgeAngle, lowerEdgeAngle filled for supercell (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2), L2-PS shall ignore these parameters.

---

**2.3.2.21.0-9.0-8**  (ID: `12696013`)

Beam Configuration update
ulBeamIdPatternIdMappingList
