### 2.3.2.22 Cell PMI Beam Data Set

#### 2.3.2.22.0-2 Cell PMI Beam Data Set Overview (ID: 10972310)

**2.3.2.22.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10972316`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
Messages:

PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq/Resp

Purpose:

To setup a cell in 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Cell Setup is done

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_795 (for cell setup), 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_57431 (for cell reconfiguration), 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1292 (Cell PMI beam data set procedure)

---

#### 2.3.2.22.0-3 Cell PMI Beam Data Set Description (ID: 10972321)

**2.3.2.22.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `12655982`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
This message is used for CPRT to send PMI beam setting data which is needed for cell with dlMimoMode set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 or with actDlSrsSubbandBm enabled to L2-PS, which usually very large (i.e. tens of kilo bytes or more) and not capable to be held in PsCell\_CellSetupReq according to SYSCOM message size limitation (Max. 64 KB). For beam update as:

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.tiltOffset,

[CB014301-A]

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle,

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.lowerEdgeAngle,

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle,

NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet.upperEdgeAngle,

[End CB014301-A]

online change, if bellow beam setting data is impacted, the update is passed by PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq from CPRT to L2PS. If needed, CPRT must split PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq into several messages, each is not larger than 64 KB.

If CL 8x4 MIMO is enabled and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false,

·A bunch of PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq messages sending following PsCell\_CellSetupReq message is mandatory, let’s call it **Primary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq. Following IEs must be present in Primary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq:**

o    beamMapping

o    correlationTable2

·Further PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message sending may also happen per NIDD configuration, let’s call it **Secondary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq. The message is used to send the following IE:**

o    eirpControlConfigExt::BeamWeight

o    eirpControlConfigExt::DftBeamRespone

During cell setup procedure, if actExternalAntennaBF is FALSE, Secondary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq with eirpControlConfigExt::BeamWeight is mandatory.

o    if actEirpControl is TRUE, another Secondary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message with eirpControlConfigExt::DftBeamRespone is also mandatory.

Else if actDlSrsSubbandBm is true and actEirpControl is true,

PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message with eirpControlConfigExt::DftBeamRespone is mandatory.

During cell reconfiguration procedure and in case of actExternalAntennaBF is FALSE, if any of following condition is satisfied, Secondary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq with eirpControlConfigExt::DftBeamRespone is also mandatory:

o    actEirpControl is changed from FALSE to TRUE

o    In case of actEirpControl is TRUE, numberOfCellSegments value is changed

**Note: Secondary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message sending is also delayed per CPRT implementation.**

---

#### 2.3.2.22.0-4 Cell PMI Beam Data Set Message validation (ID: 12690440)

**2.3.2.22.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10972347`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
Upon reception of the PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_4657\_replaced([10972358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuKSPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.3.2.22.0-5 Cell PMI Beam Data Set Concurrency handling (ID: 12690443)

**2.3.2.22.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10972352`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
Concurrent Cell PMI Beam Data Setting procedures are not managed at L2-RT side.

If a Cell PMI Beam Data Setting is initiated by 5G-CP-RT, no other PMI Beam Data Setting procedures shall be concurrently initiated, until the on-going Cell PMI Beam Data Setting procedure is Completed or Aborted.

---

#### 2.3.2.22.0-6 Cell PMI Beam Data Set Exceptions (ID: 10972358)

**2.3.2.22.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10972369`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause = InvalidParameter if:

* nrCellGrpId IE is not valid or nrCellIdentity IE is not valid or;
* totalElements IE is not equal to (numOfPmiBeams \* (numOfPmiBeams-1)/2) defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_318\_replaced([10972440](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuxRvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or;
* not all the PMI beam correlation data is received after the reception of last PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message;
* [PR684964]actEirpControl is FALSE recevied in PsCell\_CellSetupReq (defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq(defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and eirpContro4SrsDftBeam present in PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq.[End PR684964]

In case of the Primary PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq (defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_2458\_replaced([10972321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuKM_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) validation failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk". This is to indicate that rollback is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

---

#### 2.3.2.22.0-9 Cell PMI Beam Data Set IE Definitions (ID: 12690447)

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `10972401`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
**eirpControlConfigExt structure content**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameters** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| numOfTrxPerPolarization | 1..32 | M | number of TRXs in each polarization | 5GC002200-C |
| **[Before CNI-89884-A]PmiBeamData**[CNI-89884-A]pmiBeamData**[End CNI-89884-A]**\*\*\*\* | **[Before CNI-89884-A]union{** BeamWeight, DftBeamResponse **[CNI-89884-A] beamWeightOrResponse (A structure, see separate definition in 5G\_L2\_IF\_4381\_replaced([10972408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuxQfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[End CNI-89884-A]**}**\*\*\*\* | M | See the corresponding definition | 5GC002200-C |

The message with eirpControlConfigExt content is used for calculating cell's normalizedBeamGain. The size of BeamWeight is (448 + 32) \* 32 \* 4 = 61,440 bytes, and the size of DftBeamResponse is 60 \* 32 \* 4 = 7,680 bytes. The total size of BeamWeight and DftBeamResponse is larger than max SYSCOM buffer, so they are  sent in two different message.

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-5**  (ID: `12690457`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
correlationTable2

---

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12706098`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
**correlationTable2 structure content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameters | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| [Before CNI-134949-A] numOfPmiBeams [End CNI-134949-A] | 1..476 | M | number of PMI beams. Note: all PMI beams due to be used for PDCCH, PDSCH and CSI-RS sending are counted. | 5GC000524-L |
| totalElements | U32 | M | The total number of elements of PMI Beam Correlation data. [Before CNI-134949-A] This IE shall be set to numOfPmiBeams \*(numOfPmiBeams-1)/2 [End CNI-134949-A] | 5GC000524-L |
| startElementIndex | U32 | M | Start element index of PMI Beam Correlation data being indicated in data[]. Valid value: 0..(totalElements-1) | 5GC000524-L |
| [Before CNI-134949-A] numOfElements [End CNI-134949-A] | U32 | M | Number of PMI Beam Correlation elements included in data[]. Valid value: 1..(totalElements -startElementIndex) | 5GC000524-L |
| data[] | [Before CNI-134949-A] U8 array of numOfElements elements. [CNI-134949-A] U8 [1..(totalElements -startElementIndex - 1)] [End CNI-134949-A] | M | Correlation table. Formatted in a 1-D array with 8-bit unsigned integer values as specified in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2644\_replaced([11302499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfubfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | 5GC000524-L |

[CNI-134949-A]  
Note:  
numOfElements used below means size of data array.  
numPmiBeam maximum value used below is 476.  
[End CNI-134949-A]

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, the correlationTable (1-D array) is structured in the manner specified by 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2644\_replaced([11302499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfubfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with a maximum size of *numPmiBeam*(numPmiBeam/2)*8 bits = numPmiBeam*(numPmiBeam-1)/2) bytes 476*(476-1)/2 bytes =* 113,050 bytes. According to SYSCOM message size limitation, the size of each PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message can not be larger than **64 kilobytes, in order to inform the PMI Beam Correlation data indicated by correlationTable (1-D array) to L2-PS, at least two PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq messages are needed where each PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message contains only part of correlationTable (1-D array) information. The definition of correlationTable2 (structure) IE allows partial correlationTable (1-D array) data being held within one PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message, and the totalElements, startElementIndex  and numOfElements IEs of it are used to indicate whether whole correlationTable (1-D array) is included in correlationTable2 (structure) or which part of correlationTable (1-D array) is included in correlationTable2 (structure):**\*\*

 IF (startElementIndex == 0) AND (startElementIndex + numOfElements == totalElements), THEN all PMI Beam Correlation data is included in correlationTable2 data

 IF (startElementIndex == 0) AND (startElementIndex + numOfElements < totalElements), then the first part of PMI Beam Correlation data is included in correlationTable2 data

 IF (startElementIndex > 0) AND (startElementIndex + numOfElements == totalElements), then the last part of PMI Beam Correlation data is included in correlationTable2 data

 IF (startElementIndex > 0) AND (startElementIndex+numOfElements < totalElements), then (one of the) middle part of PMI Beam Correlation data is included in correlationTable2 data

In case of PMI Beam Correlation data indicated by correlationTable (1-D array) being sent with more than one PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message, PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq must be sent in correlationTable2::startElementIndex ascending order. As SYSCOM message transfer is reliable and SYSCOM message sequence is assured by platform, upon the reception of PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message with last PMI Beam Correlation data part (i.e. startElementIndex + numOfElements == totalElements), L2-PS knows that there is no PMI Beam Correlation data pending (i.e. all PMI Beam Correlation data is received). If not all PMI Beam Correlation data is received after the reception of last PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message (refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_2379\_replaced([10972376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UuKS_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about how to determine whether a PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message is the last one or not), L2-PS shall responses ‘NOK’ to client via PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetResp.

---

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-6**  (ID: `12690460`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
beamMapping

---

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12703413`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
**beamMapping structure content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameters | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| [Before CNI-134949-A] numOfPmiBeams [End CNI-134949-A] | 1..476 | M | number of PMI beams. Note: all PMI beams due to be used for PDCCH, PDSCH and CSI-RS sending are counted. | 5GC002200-D |
| ssbBeamId[] | [Before CNI-134949-A] U8 [0..63] array of numOfPmiBeams elements. [CNI-134949-A] U8 [0..475] [End CNI-134949-A] | M | correlated SSB beam ID of each PMI beam, array index is the pattern ID offset of each PMI beam. For value definition of this IE, see [5G\_UP\_ALG\_11982] and [5G\_UP\_ALG\_1937] | 5GC002200-D |

The message with beamMapping content is mapping relationship between SSB beam index and PMI beam. Details algorithm see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2517\_replaced([11294511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqDplvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-7**  (ID: `10972452`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set
**eirpControlForSrsDftBeam**

---

**2.3.2.22.0-9.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `10972476`)

Cell PMI Beam Data Set

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| dftBeamSetId | uint8[1, 2, 4] | M | Identity of current dft beam set. Should be aligned with bfSetup.dftBeamSetList.dftBeamSetId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_115\_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).   dftBeamSetId 1 is reserved for normal oversampled DFT beams for UL and DL; dftBeamSetId 2 is reserved for tapering oversampled DFT beams for DL. dftBeamSetId 4 is reserved for normal DL DFT beams for mMIMO cell (isCellMassiveMimo = True (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) in the reducedEnergySaving state (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2735\_replaced([10973678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U2tGfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). | CB008305-C |
| numOfSrsDftBeam | 1..512 | M | number of SRS DFT beams. | CB008247-D |
| normalizedBeamGain[] array of numOfSrsDftBeam\*numberOfCellSegments | 16 bit fixed point | M | Normalized SRS beam gain per cell segment shall be provided in Q1.15 linear scale. 1 value corresponds to maxBeamGain. | CB008247-D |

The message with eirpContro4SrsDftBeam content is used for SRS beam EIRP control. The maximum size of normalizedBeamGain is 60 \* 512 \* 2 = 61,440 bytes. The total size of SRS normalizedBeamGain almost reach to max SYSCOM buffer, so they are sent via seperate union struct in PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq.

In case of **[Before CB013098-C] DL MUMIMO enhancement enabled (actDlMuMimoEnh=True)** [CB013098-C] downlink SRS based beam management is actived (actDlSrsBm=true) **[End CB013098-C] and tapering enabled** (dlMuMimoTaperingH>0 and/or dlMuMimoTaperingV>0) , two PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message is need to send, one for non-tapering DFT beam with dftBeamSetId=1 and another one for tapering DFT beam with dftBeamSetId=2.  
If the cell can be a subject for massive MIMO muting for energy efficiency (see 5G\_L3\_15819), then additional PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message is needed for normal DL DFT beams for mMIMO cell in the reducedEnergySaving state with dftBeamSetId=4.  
**[CB013098-C]*****\****\*

Note:

If actDlSrsBm=true, but dlMuMimoTaperingH is not existed in NIDD, then default 25db will be used to generate tapering dft beam and calculate normalizedBeamGain . The relatated configuration  results  will send to L2PS (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4849\_replaced([11294877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqE3pPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[End CB013098-C]**

---

### 2.3.2.23 NrRel PCell Setup

#### 2.3.2.23.0-2 NrRel PCell Setup Overview (ID: 10972500)

**2.3.2.23.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `10972518`)

NrRel PCell Setup
Messages:

PsCell\_NrRelPCellSetupReq/Resp

Purpose:

When Primary and Secondary cells are not part of the same CellGroup and NrRel is learned from first corresponding Scell addition, the procedures configure Secondary cell with Primary cell's parameters.

Precondition:

Both cells have been setup in User Plane and such NrRel isn't already setup between them.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the 5G-L2-PS (SCell) address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_15161 for intra-gNB CA

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_60155 for inter-gNB CA SCell

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_60186 for inter-gNB CA PCell

[CB008140-GD]

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2386\_replaced([11179132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BebnmPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for inter-gNB CA

[End CB008140-GD]

---

#### 2.3.2.23.0-3 NrRel PCell Setup Description (ID: 10972523)

**2.3.2.23.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10972528`)

NrRel PCell Setup
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall create the requested Primary cell context and its association to the Secondary cell.

---

#### 2.3.2.23.0-4 NrRel PCell Setup Message validation (ID: 10972534)

**2.3.2.23.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10972539`)

NrRel PCell Setup
Upon reception of the PsCell\_NrRelPCellSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_NrRelPCellSetupResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the cell was setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2538\_replaced([10972545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UvYWfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.23.0-5 NrRel PCell Setup Exceptions (ID: 10972545)

**2.3.2.23.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10972552`)

NrRel PCell Setup
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_NrRelPCellSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* sCellNrCellIdentity IE is not valid, cause ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist is used, or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not allocated successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS. Clean-up is done with the L2-RT NrRel CellDelete procedure, see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_118\_replaced([11179376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bec1yvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

NrRel SCell Setup
Upon reception of the PsCell\_NrRelSCellSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

#### 2.3.2.24.0-5 NrRel SCell Setup Exceptions (ID: 10972667)

**2.3.2.24.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `10972679`)

NrRel SCell Setup
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_NrRelSCellSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* pCellNrCellIdentity IE is not valid, cause ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist is used, or;
* [Before 5GC001729-A]Flag actInterNumerologyCa is False for pCell, cause ECause5G\_InvalidParameter is used , or;[End 5GC001729-A]
* message psPeerCtrl\_NrRelPCellUpdateResp is KO, or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not allocated successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS. Clean-up is done with the L2-RT NrRel CellDelete procedure, see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_118\_replaced([11179376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bec1yvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

| >n1n2 | ENUMERATED {config4x1: 0; config2x2: 1; config8x2: 2} | M | N1N2 configuration of 38.214. 0: 4x1 (i.e. N1=4, N2=1) 1: 2x2 (i.e. N1=2, N2=2) [CB008577-D]2: 8x2 (i.e. N1=8, N2=2) [End C008577-D] If dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4[CB008577-D] or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_32x4[End CB008577-D], this IE is present. Otherwise, this IE is not present. | FGCR-11189 FGCR-12126 |
| >numOfResource | U8 [0..4] | M | Number of CSI-RS resources per resource set. Value setting restrictions: if dlMimoMode is ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4: CSI-RS resource set #1: 1 CSI-RS resource set #2: 2 CSI-RS resource set #3: 4 If actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is TRUE AND numOfSubSectors = 0: CSI-RS resource set #1: 1 CSI-RS resource set #2: 0 CSI-RS resource set #3: 0 If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks < 5: CSI-RS resource set #1: 1 CSI-RS resource set #2: 0 CSI-RS resource set #3: 0 If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks = 6: CSI-RS resource set #1: 0 CSI-RS resource set #2: 0 CSI-RS resource set #3: 4 [CB008577-D] If actBeamforming = TRUE for FDD cell and dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_32x4: CSI-RS resource set #1: 1 CSI-RS resource set #2: 1 CSI-RS resource set #3: 0 [End CB008577-D] | CB007601-A |
| sCellDlIgnbCaDestAddress | XpAddress, 5G\_L2\_IF\_249 | O | Destination address for Xp communication for IgNb CA   Only needed for inter-gNB CA. | CB008140-AC |
| srsBfSyncIndicator | ENUMERATED {NoSync: 0; SyncDlSuMimo: 1; SyncDlSuMuMimo: 2} | O | Used only if sync up is needed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_10012). If present, indicates the DL BF and the synchronization type of Pcell and Scell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2683). | CB008898-A |
| sCellRelativeBandLocation | ENUMERATED {upper\_subBand, lower\_subBand} | O | Present for intra-band FR1 UL CA. Information where secondary cell lays (in the frequency domain) versus the primary cell. | CB006449-AB |
| actDlMuMimoEnh | TRUE, FALSE | O | Activation flag for DL MU-MIMO enhancement for FR1. See definition of feature NIDD parameters.   This parameter shall be presented if srsBfSyncIndicator=1 or 2. | CB008305-A |
| taperingConfigforDlMuMimoEnh | Structure, defined 5G\_L2\_IF\_7909  [10970449: taperingConfigforDlMuMimoEnh structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjLEvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) | O | Tapering configuration for downlink MU MIMO enhancement. This parameter shall be presented if srsBfSyncIndicator=1 or 2. | CB013098-C |
| puschMappingType | ENUMERATED { 0: typeA 1: typeB } | O | Info about which puschMappingType is configured on the SCell. Present only for intra gNB FR1 T+T CA. | CB006449-CC |
| isULFragmentationEnabled | bool | O | Info, if on the SCell UL fragmentation is enabled or no. 0. Disabled 1. Enabled Present only for intra gNB FR1 T+T CA. | CB006449-CC |

As seen in requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2683, parameters numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks, actBeamforming, dlMimoMode and nrBtsBeamRefinementP2 of Scell are needed in Pcell to calculate the number of UCI bits for CSI reports.

If dlMimoMode = ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true, the UCI bits for Scell CSI reports is calculated by the following way:

* If Cell specific CSI-RS is configured for Scell UE:
* n1n2 in PsCell\_NrRelSCellSetupReq is used in the calculation for Scell UCI bits.
* Else(UE specific CSI-RS is configured for Scell UE):

n1n2 in PsCell\_NrRelSCellSetupReq is not used in the calculation for Scell UCI bits. UCI bits for 4-port CSI-RS is used for Scell UE.

---

### 2.3.2.25 NrRel PCell Delete

#### 2.3.2.25.0-2 NrRel PCell Delete Overview (ID: 10972764)

**2.3.2.25.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10972769`)

NrRel PCell Delete
Messages:

PsCell\_NrRelPCellDeleteReq/Resp

Purpose:

Delete NrRel in Secondary cell when Primary cell is deleted (or corresponding L2RT instance has crashed)

Precondition:

Secondary cell has previously received PCell configuration.

Prior to Pcell context deletion, CP-RT ensures that each related CA UE is reconfigured (Scell delete).

This Pcell deletion is not sent to Scell in case this Scell is about to be deleted (in this case, Pcell deletion is handled as part of cell deletion procedure).

Addressing:

The request is sent to the 5G-L2-PS (SCell) address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1355, 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1381

---

#### 2.3.2.25.0-3 NrRel PCell Delete Description (ID: 10972775)

**2.3.2.25.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10972778`)

NrRel PCell Delete
If several Scells in a CellGroup refer to the same Pcell context, upon reception of the request, the Pcell context is deleted when no more Scell is associated to it.

---

#### 2.3.2.25.0-4 NrRel PCell Delete Message validation (ID: 10972784)

**2.3.2.25.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10972790`)

NrRel PCell Delete
Upon reception of the PsCell\_NrRelPCellDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_NrRelPCellDeleteResp message if the request message is valid, the NR relation end point was deleted successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_4983\_replaced([10972796](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UxNgfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.25.0-5 NrRel PCell Delete Exceptions (ID: 10972796)

**2.3.2.25.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10972802`)

NrRel PCell Delete
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_ NrRelPCellDeleteResp message also if:

* sCellNrCellIdentity or pCellNrCellIdentity IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not deleted successfully.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

#### 2.3.2.25.0-6 NrRel PCell Delete PsCell_NrRelPCellDeleteReq message content (ID: 10972808)

### 2.3.2.26 NrRel SCell Delete

#### 2.3.2.26.0-2 NrRel SCell Delete Overview (ID: 10972844)

**2.3.2.26.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10972849`)

NrRel SCell Delete
Messages:

PsCell\_NrRelSCellDeleteReq/Resp

Purpose:

Delete NrRel in Primary cell when Secondary cell is deleted (or corresponding L2RT instance has crashed)

Precondition:

Primary cell has previously received Scell configuration.

Prior to Scell context deletion, CP-RT ensures that no more Ue have a leg on this Scell.

This Scell deletion is not send to Pcell in case this PCell is about to be deleted.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the 5G-L2-PS (PCell) address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1355, 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1381

### 2.3.2.27 NrRel SCell Update

#### 2.3.2.27.0-2 NrRel SCell Update Overview (ID: 13379155)

**2.3.2.27.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13379424`)

NrRel SCell Update
Messages:

PsCell\_NrRelSCellUpdateReq/Resp

Purpose:

The purpose of this procedure is to perform beamforming data synchronization due to online modification of beamSet parameters on PCell or SCell.

Precondition:

Both PCell, SCell and Nr Rel are setup.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the 5G-L2-PS (PCell) address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

L2-RT NrRel PCell/SCell Update ([13381668: L2-RT NrRel PCell/SCell Update](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Olk1IAApEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw))

#### 2.3.2.27.0-3 NrRel SCell Update Description (ID: 13379156)

**2.3.2.27.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13381700`)

NrRel SCell Update
Upon reception of the request PsCell\_NrRelSCellUpdateReq 5G-L2-PS performs beamforming data synchronization.

---

#### 2.3.2.27.0-4 NrRel SCell Update Message validation (ID: 13379157)

**2.3.2.27.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13381716`)

NrRel SCell Update
Upon reception of the PsCell\_NrRelSCellUpdateReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the message.

---

#### 2.3.2.27.0-5 NrRel SCell Update Exceptions (ID: 13379159)

**2.3.2.27.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13382277`)

NrRel SCell Update
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP ([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805 ([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806 ([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* sCellNrCellIdentity or pCellNrCellIdentity IE is not valid, cause ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist is used,
* the request message is not valid.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

### 2.3.2.28 UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics

#### 2.3.2.28.0-2 UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics Overview (ID: 10972922)

**2.3.2.28.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10972933`)

UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics
Messages:

PsCell\_TestMeasurementReq

PsCell\_TestMeasurementResp

PsCell\_UlTestMeasurementInd

PsCell\_DlTestMeasurementInd

Purpose:

Ensure the capability to perform Remote RU-diagnostics.

To provide 5G-CP-RT the requested cell test measurement, for the required processing period:

for UL cell test: based on RTWP, RSSI [CB006293]and SINR [end CB006293] information given by 5G-L1-UL, aggregated by 5G-L2-PS

for DL cell test: based on EIRP control measurement estimated TX power,  processed by 5G-L2-PS

Precondition:

the cell is setup

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

The indication message are sent to the address where the request was sent from.

---

#### 2.3.2.28.0-3 UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics Description (ID: 10972938)

**2.3.2.28.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `10972955`)

UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics
5G-L2-PS provides 5G-CP-RT requested Ul Cell test measurement per antenna, based on RTWP, RSSI and SINR information coming from 5G-UL-L1 on PUSCH traffic allocation schema [see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5275].

5G-L2-PS provides 5G-CP-RT requested Dl Cell test measurement, based on Average TX Power estimated for the Cell [see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5268].

**Constraints:**

L2-PS will not be able to handle parallel PsCell\_TestMeasurementReq/Resp procedure, 5G-CP-RT shall not initiate such parallel procedure, new PsCell\_TestMeasurementReq is delayed until previous PsCell\_TestMeasurementResp is received in 5G-CP-RT or procedure reached time-out.

L2-PS will send back PsCell\_TestMeasurementResp response message with EStatus5G\_NotOk; to any request done whereas another current Cell test measurement request processing is on-going, and until all current expected Ul/DL Cell test measurement indication message(s) have been sent to 5G-CP-RT.

L2-PS shall transmit the result in Ul/DL Cell test measurement indication message(s) no more than 30 seconds after receiving the request.

**[CB009556-B]NOTE：5G-L2-PS can use powerBudgetPerBeam from 5G\_L3\_IF\_1153 to fill IE etpPerPath for non-beamforming, as it is equivalent to ETP per path obtained from the formula according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24155.**

For non-beamforming, powerBudgetPerBeam = Max output power – 10log10(Num. of TRXs per RU) according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2550

where:

Max output power: The maximum power of the cell.

Num. of TRXs per RU: The number of MIMO streams or layers used (non-beamforming).**[End CB009556-B]**

---

#### 2.3.2.28.0-4 UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics Exceptions (ID: 10972961)

**2.3.2.28.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12772250`)

UL and DL Cell Test Measurement for remote RU-diagnostics
Expected Exceptions:

N/A

N/A

### 2.3.2.29 Cell GBR Load Indication

#### 2.3.2.29.0-1 Cell GBR Load Indication Overview (ID: 10973058)

**2.3.2.29.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10973064`)

Cell GBR Load Indication
Messages:

PsCell\_DlGbrLoadInd/ PsCell\_UlGbrLoadInd

Purpose:

Periodically report GBR PRB load and time domain load for DL or UL to CP-RT.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_1395: Cell GBR Load Information Report

---

#### 2.3.2.29.0-2 Cell GBR Load Indication Description (ID: 10973070)

**2.3.2.29.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973076`)

Cell GBR Load Indication
Through PsCell\_DlGbrLoadInd and PsCell\_UlGbrLoadInd, 5G-L2-PS reports DL/UL GBR PRB load and time domain load to CP-RT.

These two messages are transmitted periodically, the periodicity is equal to IE gbrLoadUpdatePeriod inside PsCell\_CellSetupReq or latest PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message which is received from CP-RT. When received gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is zero, these two messages won’t be transmitted.

When online modification occurs for gbrLoadUpdatePeriod, the periodicity of these two messages will also be changed accordingly. Especially, when gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is changed to zero from non-zero, the transmitting will be stopped; when gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is changed to non-zero from zero, the transmitting will be started.

NOTE: Upon reception of the Cell setup Request [5G\_L2\_IF\_49\_replaced([10966848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQ3OPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))], 5G-L2-PS shall store the address of the client (as destination address for PsCell\_DlGbrLoadInd and PsCell\_UlGbrLoadInd).

---

**2.3.2.29.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973086`)

Cell GBR Load Indication
Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

None

E.g. If 3 Dedicated BWPs are configured then 0th index is for large, 1st index is for mid and 2nd index is for small BWP. In case 2 Dedicated BWPs are configured then 0th index is for large, 1st index is for small BWP.   If the value of gbrPrbLoadPerBwp[0] or gbrPrbLoadPerBwp[1] happens to be greater than 100, L2-PS shall limit the value to 100 | CB008954-C |

### 2.3.2.33 Remote Interference indication

#### 2.3.2.33.0-2 Remote Interference indication General (ID: 10973273)

#### 2.3.2.33.1 Procedures

##### 2.3.2.33.1.0-1 Procedures Overview (ID: 10973291)

**2.3.2.33.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10973293`)

Procedures
Messages:

PsCell\_RemoteInterferenceInd

Purpose:

The purpose of this indication message is to provide information to 5G-CP-RT whether remote interference has been observed or the observation of remote interference ended.

Precondition:

This message will be sent only if PsCell\_CellSetupReq/PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq.actNrRim != "disabled".

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1584\_replaced([11179451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BedcxfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Remote Interference Indication flow

---

##### 2.3.2.33.1.0-2 Procedures Description (ID: 10973300)

**2.3.2.33.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `10973319`)

Procedures
Indication message which is used to inform 5G-CP-RT if remote interference presence has been detected and potential mitigation actions are requierd from 5G-CP-RT side. Message will be sent [Before CB014133-A] when

* state of remote interference presence is changing from State 1 -> State 2 and State 2 -> State 0 according to the detection mechanism described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9180.
* RIM RS signal detection state changed - see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9180
* RI mitigation state has changed

[CB014133-A]

at the end RI detection window

[End CB014133-A]

---

##### 2.3.2.33.1.0-3 Procedures Exceptions (ID: 10973325)

**2.3.2.33.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973331`)

Procedures
Expected Exceptions:

Unexpected Exceptions:

N/A

---

##### 2.3.2.33.1.1 PsCell_RemoteInterferenceInd

###### 2.3.2.33.1.1.0-1 PsCell_RemoteInterferenceInd PsCell_RemoteInterferenceInd message content: (ID: 10973337)

**2.3.2.33.1.1.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13337869`)

PsCell\_RemoteInterferenceInd

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| nrCellIdentity | 1...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | CB008249-A |
| remoteInterferenceDetected | bool | M | Parameter describes if Remote Interference has been detected. True - remote interference has been detected, False - remote interference isn't currently observed. | CB008249-A |
| rimRsDetected | Enum { 0: notDetected 1: Type1 2: Type2 3: Type1AndType2 } | M | Parameter describes if RIM RS is observed at the moment this indication is sent. 5G-L2-PS indicates if the RIM RS has been detected from at least single gNB. 'Type1' means only RIM RS type 1 is detected 'Type2' means only RIM RS type 2 is detected 'Type1AndType2' means both RIM RS type 1 and type 2 are detected   Once the detection stops due to e.g. lack of RI detection, configuration setting or lack of RIM RS, then this parameter will be set to 'notDetected'. | CB006991-C |
| dlPdschMuting | Enum{ noMuting, noneNoneNoneFull, noneNoneFullFull, noneFullFullFull, noneNoneFullNone, noneFullFullNone, fullFullFullFull, fullFullFullNone noneNoneNoneFour, noneNoneFourFull, noneNoneEightFull, noneFourFullFull, noneEightFullFull, fourFullFullFull, eightFullFullFull, noneNoneFourNone, noneNoneEightNone, noneFourFullNone, noneEightFullNone, fourFullFullNone, eightFullFullNone } | M | Parameter describes the type of RI DL PDSCH muting used by 5G-L2-PS at the moment this indication is sent. Muting is described by providing the status of each slot in time order respectively, i.e. 3rd DL slot before Special Slot on the left, then 2nd DL slot before SS, then 1st DL slot before SS and SS on the right. Sub-value ‘none’ means there is no PDSCH muting in the slot, ‘full’ means all PDSCH symbols are muted in the slot, ‘four’ means last four PDSCH symbols are muted in the slot, ‘eight’ means last eight PDSCH symbols are muted in the slot  In case of pattern with 2 different number of DL symbols in BI slot, the maximum value is reported e.g. for one BI slot we have: noneNoneNoneFull,  for 2nd BI slot we have:  noneNoneFullFull, then noneNoneFullFull is reported L2PS shall not report noMuting state caused by RI pilot processing. Instead previous state (one just before unmuting caused by RI pilot processing) is reported. It is done to avoid reporting status change too often. | CB006991-D |
| [Before CB013330-A] dlPdcchMuting [End CB013330-A] | [Before CB013330-A] bool [End CB013330-A] | [Before CB013330-A] M [End CB013330-A] | [Before CB013330-A] Parameter defines if DL PDCCH muting is applied. L2PS shall not report false state caused by RI pilot processing. Instead previous state (one just before unmuting caused by RI pilot processing) is reported. It is done to avoid reporting status change too often.  [End CB013330-A] | [Before CB013330-A] PR780165 [End CB013330-A] |
| dlPdcchMutingStatus | Enum: 0: noMuting 1: specialSlotMuting 2: specialAndPreviousSlotMuting 3: specialAndTwoPreviousSlotMuting | M | Parameter defines status of DL PDCCH muting. L2PS shall not report disabled state caused by RI pilot processing. Instead previous state (one just before unmuting caused by RI pilot processing) is reported. It is done to avoid reporting status change too often. | CB013330-A |
| rimAsymmetricStatus | Enum{nonAsymmetric, asymmetric} | M | L2PS needs to update the "Asymmetric" or "NonAsymmetric" status according to algorithm 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24447. nonAsymmetric is default value | CB009823-D |
| rimRs1DetectedSetIds [MAX\_SET\_IDS] | List of U32 | M | List of Set ID values from currently detected RIM RS type 1 signals. MAX\_SET\_IDS: Size of list is dynamic, based on NIDD parameter (PsCell\_CellSetupReq.rimRsConfig.rimRsSetidListLength, please see 5G\_L2\_IF\_8023\_replaced(10970065)), but maximum upper limit is 640. SetIDs on list are always sorted in descending order, starting from setId with highest power. | 03851885 |
| rimRs2DetectedSetIds [MAX\_SET\_IDS] | List of U32 | M | List of Set ID values from currently detected RIM RS type 2 signals. SetIDs on list are always sorted in descending order, starting from setId with highest power. | 03851885 |

| nrRiThresBasePerSubband | Array of int16, [1...5], -120...-60 | M | This array indicates the calculated base threshold of interference power level per RB in uplink symbols for remote interference detection for each subband. Each index in array indicates threshold for different subband, where:  [0] - subband ... [4] - subband4 Amount of elements in the array which are provided by L2PS shall match number of configured subbands on NRCELL. | CB014613-A |

### 2.3.2.34 Rim Rs indication

#### 2.3.2.34.0-2 Rim Rs indication General (ID: 10973405)

#### 2.3.2.34.1 Procedures

##### 2.3.2.34.1.0-1 Procedures Overview (ID: 10973422)

**2.3.2.34.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10973427`)

Procedures
[Before 05101473]

**Messages:**

PsCell\_RimRsIndication

**Purpose:**

The purpose of this indication message is to provide information to 5G-CP-RT whether Rim Rs signal has been observed or the observation of Rim Rs signal ended.

**Precondition:**

This message will be sent only if PsCell\_CellSetupReq/PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq.actNrRim == "framework0" or "framework1".

**Addressing:**

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

[End 05101473]

Changes: Message removed by pronto 05101473. Content of the messaged merged to [10973285: PsCell\_RemoteInterferenceInd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U0Q1Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

##### 2.3.2.34.1.0-2 Procedures Description (ID: 10973433)

**2.3.2.34.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973439`)

Procedures
[Before 05101473]

Indication message which is used to inform 5G-CP-RT if Rim Rs signal has been detected. Message will be sent:

[Before CB014133-A-UPD3]

Framework0:  at the end of every n’th RIM-RS transmission period, where n is equal to rdRimRsUpdateInterval (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32376)

Framework1: at the end of every n’th RS1 transmission period for RIM-RS1 and at the end of every n’th RS2 transmission period for RIM-RS2 respectively, where n is equal to rdRimRsUpdateInterval (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32376) (message will be send twice in every n’th RIM RS transmission period in framework1).

[CB014133-A-UPD3]

At the end of every RI detection window.

[End CB014133-A-UPD3]

For details see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32391.

[End 05101473]

Changes: Message removed by pronto 05101473. Content of the messaged merged to [10973285: PsCell\_RemoteInterferenceInd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U0Q1Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

### 2.3.2.35 IgNB CA Cell Create

#### 2.3.2.35.0-2 IgNB CA Cell Create Overview (ID: 10973480)

**2.3.2.35.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973486`)

IgNB CA Cell Create
Messages:

[Before PR656432]PsCell\_IgNbCaCellCreateReq/Resp[PR656432]PsCell\_IgnbCaCellCreateReq/Resp[End PR656432]

Purpose:

To exchange information related to Xp header and 5G-L2-PS EQID address.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSC:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_59478

---

#### 2.3.2.35.0-3 IgNB CA Cell Create Description (ID: 10973491)

**2.3.2.35.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973497`)

IgNB CA Cell Create
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall store the DL XpIf CA Routing Data in DL scheduler's cell database for use when sending messages to XpIf.

5G-L2-PS shall respond with own EQID address used for communication with XpIf, see 5G\_L2\_2842\_replaced([11140255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23iaBfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 2.3.2.37 Cell Power Saving Configuration

#### 2.3.2.37.0-2 Cell Power Saving Configuration Overview (ID: 10973624)

**2.3.2.37.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13327684`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
**Messages:**

PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To configure:

* online-modifiable power saving options for a given 5G-L2-PS cell
* load-based MIMO muting for Energy Efficiency
* [CB014095-B] online massive MIMO muting FR1 for energy efficiency [End CB014095-B]

**Precondition:**

Cell exists.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant MSCs:**

* 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_63409: TX Switch Off for Energy Saving
* 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_63720: TX Switch On for Non-Energy Saving
* [CB014095-B] [12770633:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Z6kEi4iVEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) Online Activate Cell Load Measurement for mMIMO TX Power Saving [End CB014095-B]

---

#### 2.3.2.37.0-3 Cell Power Saving Configuration Description (ID: 10973633)

**2.3.2.37.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973637`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update cell context for the online-modifiable parameters contained in the message and all related resources.

This request message contains information elements which are updated:

* as a result of the execution of power-saving algorithms in 5G-CP-RT,
* irrespectively of any reconfiguration action performed by an operator or a Self-Organizing Network.

---

#### 2.3.2.37.0-4 Cell Power Saving Configuration Message Validation (ID: 10973642)

**2.3.2.37.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10973647`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
Upon reception of the PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationResp message and set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok if the request message is valid and the power saving parameters were configured successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2733\_replaced([10973652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U2tFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.37.0-5 Cell Power Saving Configuration Exceptions (ID: 10973652)

**2.3.2.37.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10973657`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
Generic handling

---

**2.3.2.37.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10973663`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If a cell with a given nrCellGrpId IE and nrCellIdentity IE is not known, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

---

**2.3.2.37.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `10973667`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
Artificial-load-specific

---

**2.3.2.37.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973672`)

Cell Power Saving Configuration
When PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationReq message is received for the given cell and the energySavingState IE is set to reducedEnergySaving, 5G-L2-PS shall access the artificialLoadInfo structure (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_111\_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from the latest PsCell\_CellSetupReq/PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message content.

If patternIdsForArtificialLoadForEmfTestMode list is NOT empty and emfTotalTargetLoad is greater than 0, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* respond with PsCell\_PowerSavingConfigurationResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidOperation.

Rationale: The cell shall not enter reducedEnergySaving state when DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation is enabled.

---

### 2.3.2.38 IgNB Xp Link Status Indication

#### 2.3.2.38.0-2 IgNB Xp Link Status Indication Overview (ID: 10973723)

**2.3.2.38.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973727`)

IgNB Xp Link Status Indication
Messages:

PsCell\_IgnbXpLinkStatusInd

Purpose:

To inform local CP-RT about detected Xp-U link status

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

Relevant UP MSC:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_64266

---

#### 2.3.2.38.0-3 IgNB Xp Link Status Indication Description (ID: 10973733)

**2.3.2.38.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973738`)

IgNB Xp Link Status Indication
Indication message which is used to inform local 5G-CP-RT about Xp-U link status. Message will be sent when:

* PCell changes the Xp-U link state to unavailable (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12815)
* PCell considers the Xp-U link as recovered and changes its Xp-U link state to available (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14019)
* PCell receives from ext-SCell an indication about the Xp-U link status (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12816)

---

### 2.3.2.39 Cell Non GBR Load Indication

#### 2.3.2.39.0-1 Cell Non GBR Load Indication Overview (ID: 10973769)

**2.3.2.39.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10973772`)

Cell Non GBR Load Indication
Messages:

PsCell\_UlNonGbrLoadInd

Purpose:

Periodically report non GBR PRB load for UL to CP-RT.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsCell\_CellClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

---

#### 2.3.2.39.0-2 Cell Non GBR Load Indication Description (ID: 10973778)

**2.3.2.39.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973783`)

Cell Non GBR Load Indication
PsCell\_UlNonGbrLoadInd periodically report non GBR PRB [CB008124-H-UPD001] and TBS [End CB008124-H-UPD001] load for UL to CP-RT. [CB008124-H-UPD001] This message shall send after GBR load report message PsCell\_UlGbrLoadInd defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_363\_replaced([10973053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uybrfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008124-H-UPD001]

The periodicity is equal to IE gbrLoadUpdatePeriod inside PsCell\_CellSetupReq or latest PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message which is received from CP-RT. When received gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is zero, report won’t be transmitted.

When online modification occurs for gbrLoadUpdatePeriod, the periodicity of report will also be changed accordingly. Especially, when gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is changed to zero from non-zero, the transmitting will be stopped; when gbrLoadUpdatePeriod is changed to non-zero from zero, the transmitting will be started.

---

Expected Exceptions:

Unexpected Exceptions:

### 2.3.2.40 UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control

#### 2.3.2.40.0-2 UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control Overview (ID: 10973824)

**2.3.2.40.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10973829`)

UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control
Messages:

PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlReq/Resp

Purpose:

CP-RT use this message notify L2-PS to suspend or resume UL configured grant type2 activation process.

Precondition:

Cell exists and UL CG type2 enabled on cell.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

---

#### 2.3.2.40.0-3 UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control Description (ID: 10973836)

**2.3.2.40.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973840`)

UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update cell level CG activation control flags specified in 5G\_L2\_12197\_replaced([11176727](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_262MtfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlResp message and set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok if cell context update successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_4615\_replaced([10973847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U37Ovu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.40.0-4 UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control Exceptions (ID: 10973847)

**2.3.2.40.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12732094`)

UL Configured Grant Type2 Activation Control
**Expected Exceptions:**

Generic exception handling rules can be found in 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If a cell with a given nrCellGrpId IE and nrCellIdentity IE is not known, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist

[CB008250-F]

If UL Plmn Aware Scheduler is activated ([10969903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ufgu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ulCgType2ActivationControl IE is set, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter

If UL Plmn Aware Scheduler is not activated and ulCgType2ActivationControlPerPlmn IE is not empty, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter

If plmnId IE within ulCgType2ActivationControlPerPlmn IE is set to value not configured in Cell Setup([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_UlCGType2ActivationControlResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist

[End CB008250-F]

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

None.

---

#### 2.3.2.41 Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling

##### 2.3.2.41.0-2 Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling Overview (ID: 10973910)

**2.3.2.41.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13462407`)

Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling
**Messages:**

PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

CP-RT uses this message to notify L2-PS to update slot blanking/muting parameters for RF Cooling

**Precondition:**

Cell exists and parameter allowGBRMutingForRfCooling is configured on the cell.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs: [Before CNI-157588-A]TBD[CNI-157588-A][13462379: RF Cooling or Slot Blanking Configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_631ZdDMQEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)[End CNI-157588-A]**

---

##### 2.3.2.41.0-3 Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling Description (ID: 10973920)

**2.3.2.41.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10973925`)

Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update cell level RF cooling parameters. Slot muting shall start/stop/modify immediately as per the configuration indicated in the PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq message.  5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message and set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok and cause IE = ECause5G\_Ok if cell context is updated successfully.

Message handling details

1) rfCoolingMode = True indicates that the RFCoolingMode needs to be applied and slot blanking has to be started with target muting ration as indicated in the parameter tgtMutingRatio.

2) rfCoolingMode = False indicates that the RFCoolingMode needs to be removed and slot blanking has to be stopped. Other parameters may be ignored OR not to be read in this case.

---

##### 2.3.2.41.0-4 Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling Exceptions (ID: 10973930)

**2.3.2.41.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `10973949`)

Slot blanking/muting parameter configuration for RF Cooling
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

1) If a cell with a given nrCellGrpId IE and nrCellIdentity IE is not known, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* not reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message
* no status change at L2-PS

Unexpected Exceptions:

1) When rfCoolingMode = true and optional parameter tgtMutingRatio is not included in PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter.

2) When rfCoolingMode = true and optional parameter tgtMutingRatio set to value 0 or greater than 100 in PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,

and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter.

3) When rfCoolingMode = true in PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq message and corresponding cell is [Before CB011114-A] not for FR1 TDD [CB011114-A] FR2 TDD [End CB011114-A], 5G-L2-PS shall:

* reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,

and set cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter.

4) When rfCoolingMode = true and optional parameter rfUnitSharedWithAnotherCell is not included in PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* assume the rfUnitSharedWithAnotherCell = false (indicating its a single cell case)
* reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_Ok.

5) When rfCoolingMode = true and all other parameters are same as existing configuration, 5G-L2-PS shall:

* maintain the same configuration for all parameters
* reply with PsCell\_SlotBlankingResp message,
* set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok
* and set cause IE = ECause5G\_Ok.

---

### 2.3.2.42 Antennas TRX status indication

#### 2.3.2.42.0-2 Antennas TRX status indication Overview (ID: 10974006)

**2.3.2.42.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10974015`)

Antennas TRX status indication
Messages:

PsCell\_AntStatusBitmapInd

Purpose:

To inform 5G-L2-PS about broken Tx/Rx pipes.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the 5G-L2-PS address.

Relevant UP MSC:

Note: [CB009527-A] In ECPRI 7-2e, (See 5G\_L2\_18130\_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

L2PS doesn't expect CP indicate broken TRX through this message anymore. becasue  The broken antenna (TRX) for SB BF shall be directly handled by RF SW and L1 Radio. 5G-L2-PS doesn't need to know any information about broken antenna (TRX) because related processing for SRS CE and BWVs with broken antenna(s) can be internally handled by L1 Radio.  refering 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22217 [End CB009527-A]

---

#### 2.3.2.42.0-3 Antennas TRX status indication Description (ID: 10974021)

**2.3.2.42.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10974026`)

Antennas TRX status indication
Upon reception of the indication, 5G-L2-PS needs to update the broken information of the transmitting and receiving antennas separately. 5G-L2-PS converts the Tx bitmap and Rx bitmap to a single TRxbitmap and forwards it to ULPHY via UlData\_SrsReceiveReq(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_235\_replaced([11514315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oW_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Message handling details

1) direction = Tx indicates Tx bitmap need update.

2) direction = Rx indicates Rx bitmap need update.

---

#### 2.3.2.42.0-4 Antennas TRX status indication Exceptions (ID: 10974032)

**2.3.2.42.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10974037`)

Antennas TRX status indication
Expected Exceptions:

Unexpected Exceptions:

---

### 2.3.2.44 Sync Status Indication

#### 2.3.2.44.0-2 Sync Status Indication Overview (ID: 10974150)

**2.3.2.44.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10974156`)

Sync Status Indication
Messages:

PsCell\_SyncStatusInd

Direction:

5G-CP-RT -> 5G-L2-PS

Purpose:

To inform 5G-L2-PS about detected synchronization status change.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The indication is sent to the PsCell address.

Relevant UP MSC:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_4810\_replaced([11196908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf3K__vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.3.2.44.0-3 Sync Status Indication Description (ID: 10974162)

**2.3.2.44.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10974169`)

Sync Status Indication
Message shall be sent:

 only once for each syncStatus change, and,

 only to cell which has at least one inter-gNB CA relation established.

Upon reception of the valid (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_5893\_replaced([10974175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U6Xdfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to check message exceptions) PsCell\_SyncStatusInd message, the 5G-L2-PS shall follow 5G\_L2\_16178\_replaced([11143775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2318EPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.44.0-4 Sync Status Indication Exceptions (ID: 10974175)

**2.3.2.44.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10974179`)

Sync Status Indication
**Expected Exceptions:**

Upon reception of:

 redundant PsCell\_SyncStatusInd message, i.e., *syncStatus value is the same as in previously received PsCell\_SyncStatusInd,*

 incorrectly addressed PsCell\_SyncStatusInd message, i.e., received by cell which doesn’t have inter-gNB CA relations,

then the 5G-L2-PS instance shall raise dedicated warning.

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

---

| syncStatus | ENUMERATED {InSync; OutOfSync} | M | It is set to InSync if synchronization criteria of gNB-DU for phase dependent feature is met so that inter-gNB CA (CB008140) can be activated (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24836); or OutOfSync otherwise (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24835). See 5G\_CP\_IF\_NTW\_13341. | CB008451-C-UPD001 |

##### 2.3.2.45 Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication

Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication
**Messages:**

[Before CB008577-D]

[CB008577-D]

[End CB008577-D]

To indicate the degree of angle of SSB/refine [CB008577-D] or full sector SSB/beamset#4/FDD PMI[End CB008577-D] beams to 5G-L2-PS.

**Addressing:**

###### 2.3.2.45.0-3 Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication Description (ID: 10974218)

**2.3.2.45.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13327716`)

Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication
This message is used for CPRT to send SSB/refine [CB008577-D]or FDD PMI[End CB008577-D] beam degree of angle to L2-PS, which usually large and not capable to be held in PsCell\_CellSetupReq according to SYSCOM message size limitation (Max. 64 KB).

---

###### 2.3.2.45.0-4 Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication Exceptions (ID: 10974228)

**2.3.2.45.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13327732`)

Cell SSB/refine/PMI Beam DOA Indication
**Expected Exceptions:**

5G-L2-PS shall raise dedicated warning if:

* nrCellGrpId IE is not valid or nrCellIdentity IE is not valid or;
* size of ssbRefineBeamDoA IE is not equal to the size of beamWeightVector(beamWeightVector is received from CPRT in PsCell\_CellSetupReq)(5G\_L2\_IF\_115\_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008577-D] for TDD beamforming cell, and size for FDD beamforming cell shall be as per [10974241: PsCell\_CellSsbRefineBeamDoaInd/PsCell\_CellSsbRefinePmiBeamDoaInd(renamed from CB008577-D) message content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U6-gvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).[End CB008577-D]

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

---

| [Before CB008577-D] >>doaV[] [End C008577-D] | int16(Q8) | M | Degree of vertical angle. Q8 precision. | CB010986-C |
| [CB008577-D] pmiBeamDoA [End CB008577-D] | Structure DoaInfo [1296] DoaInfo is structure as [13367674: DoaInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_WqxtsPdBEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) | M | dynamic array of pmi beam DOA: first 16 DOA is for 8 port CSI-RS PMI beam, next 256 DOA is for 32 port CSI-RS rank1/2 PMI beam, the last 1024 DOA is for 32 port CSI-RS rank3/4 PMI beam. The DOA sequence of each type of PMI shall be the same as each kind of patternId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq->bfSetupFdd. It is for FDD cell with actBeamforming = TRUE, otherwise the size of the array shall be 0. | CB008577-D |

### 2.3.2.46 Overload Protection

#### 2.3.2.46.0-2 Overload Protection Overview (ID: 10974266)

**2.3.2.46.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10974271`)

Overload Protection
Messages:

PsCell\_OverloadProtectionReq/Resp

Purpose:

To indicate C-Plane that L2-PS is in overload state in a L2 pool and/or at L2 cell level.

Precondition:

Cell exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

N/A

---

#### 2.3.2.46.0-3 Overload Protection Description (ID: 10974277)

**2.3.2.46.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10974282`)

Overload Protection
The purpose of this message is to inform CP-RT by L2-PS about the signalling overload in a L2Pool and/or the scheduling overload at cell level.

The Overload Protection mechanism by L2-PS shall trigger condition on the two levels. In case of exceeding the thresholds, L2-PS shall explicitly trigger overload indication to CP-RT by listed type of overload:

* The first type is signaling overload and L2-PS shall communicate on “L2 pool level” where all the cells in the pool shall be considered as overloaded by CP-RT.
* The second type is scheduling overload and L2-PS shall communicate on “cell level”.

---

#### 2.3.2.46.0-4 Overload Protection Exceptions (ID: 10974288)

**2.3.2.46.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12811408`)

Overload Protection
**Expected Exceptions:**

In case of lack the response message from CP-RT, L2-PS shall repeat the same message [Before PR851629]5 times in 200 ms interval. If no response message after 5th message then L2-PS shall drop message and logging error [PR851629] periodically according to the pattern:

min(200ms \* (rdMultiplierTimeMessageOvlProtectionReq ^ rdNumberRetransmissionsMessageOvlProtectionReq), rdMaxRetransmissionTimeMessageOvlProtectionReq)

until receive response message [End PR851629] .

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

None.

---

#### 2.3.2.46.0-5 Overload Protection PsCell_OverloadProtectionReq (ID: 10974300)

**2.3.2.46.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `10974311`)

|  |  |  |  |  |

### 2.3.2.47 Cell Artificial Load Configuration

#### 2.3.2.47.0-2 Cell Artificial Load Configuration Overview (ID: 10974345)

**2.3.2.47.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13363153`)

Cell Artificial Load Configuration
**Messages:**

PsCell\_ArtificialLoadConfigReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

To configure artificial load for a given 5G-L2-PS cell.

**Precondition:**

Cell exists.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsCell address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_82493: Sub flow - Internal Cell Setup

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_57431: Cell Reconfiguration

[CB014005-B][12538884: Beam Configuration Update](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8eFycSAoEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [End CB014005-B]

---

#### 2.3.2.47.0-3 Cell Artificial Load Configuration Description (ID: 10974357)

**2.3.2.47.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10974363`)

Cell Artificial Load Configuration
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall update cell context with the artificial load configuration parameters contained in the message and update all related resources.

---

#### 2.3.2.47.0-4 Cell Artificial Load Configuration Message Validation (ID: 10974368)

**2.3.2.47.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10974374`)

Cell Artificial Load Configuration
Upon reception of the PsCell\_ArtificialLoadConfigReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsCell\_ArtificialLoadConfigResp message and set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok if the request message is valid and the artificial load parameters were configured successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2733\_replaced([10973652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U2tFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.3.2.47.0-5 Cell Artificial Load Configuration Exceptions (ID: 10974380)

**2.3.2.47.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10974385`)

Cell Artificial Load Configuration
Generic handling

---

**2.3.2.47.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10974391`)

Cell Artificial Load Configuration
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object reconfiguration can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If a cell with a given nrCellGrpId IE and nrCellIdentity IE is not known, 5G-L2-PS shall:

• reply with PsCell\_ArtificialLoadConfigResp message,

• set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk,

• and set cause IE = ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

---

PsCell\_UlCompConfigInd

**2.3.2.48.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12794247`)

Cell UL Comp Config
CP-RT shall sent message only when all below conditions are met:

* actUlComp is set to basic (1)
* UlComp cell list has changed (cells have been added and/or removed).

Parameter is applicable for FR1. actMacResourceUtilizationCounter is a bitset with the following meaning: \* 00000000 – OFF \* 00000001 – Scheduled UEs per slot per PMQAP profile \* 00000010 – Scheduled Slot per PMQAP profile Configured by the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMCCP/actMacResourceUtilizationCounter Default value: 0 | CB012724-B |

#### 2.3.2.49.0-4 Common IEs ActNrPxschTxDistCounters (ID: 12677394)

**2.3.2.49.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12677395`)

Common IEs
ActNrPxschTxDistCounters structure content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| ActNrPxschTxDistCounters | Bitset<6> | M | Activates counting for given DRB profile based on the value of the bitset<6>: 00 0000 - the counter is not activated 00 0001 - DRB profile = HR1 00 0010 - DRB profile = HR2 00 0100 - DRB profile = BR1 00 1000 - DRB profile = BR2 01 0000 - DRB profile = none 10 0000 - DRB profile = VoNR | CB010980-E |

#### 2.3.2.49.0-5 Common IEs DlPathlossBasedRlqMeasCountersConfig (ID: 12790507)

**2.3.2.49.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12790508`)

Common IEs
DlPathlossBasedRlqMeasCountersConfig structure content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| actCellTptPerRadioLinkQualityCount | Boolean | M | This parameter activates/deactivates the DL pathloss based radio link quality performance related measurement counters. Parameter is applicable for both FR1 and FR2 cells. This parameter is set to true when NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actRadioQualityMeasCount has selected value '9' (i.e.: Cell throughput per Radio Link quality). The modified value is taken into use for all UEs (existing and newly added). | CB012268-B |
| actUeCountPerRadioLinkQualityCount | Boolean | M | This parameter activates/deactivates the DL pathloss based radio link quality performance related measurement counters. Parameter is applicable for both FR1 and FR2 cells. This parameter is set to true when NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actRadioQualityMeasCount has selected value '10' (i.e.: UE Count per Radio Link quality). The modified value is taken into use for all UEs (existing and newly added). | CB012268-B-UPD001 |
| cellEdgeUePathlossThrPmCount | Range: 41... 160 Step size: 1 Unit: dB | O | This parameter sets the threshold for identifying cell-edge UEs based on their downlink pathloss. Parameter is applicable for both FR1 and FR2 cells. CP-RT always configures this parameter when 'actCellTptPerRadioLinkQualityCount' [CB012268-B-UPD001]or 'actUeCountPerRadioLinkQualityCount' [End CB012268-B-UPD001] is enabled. Configured by the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/NRPMCCP\_CELL/cellEdgeUePathlossThrPmCount. Default value: 120 The online modified value is taken into use for all UEs (existing and newly added) Note: a) Due to the functionality introduced in CB013033, any optional NIDD parameter with a default value shall be configured towards L2-PS using its default value. | CB012268-B |
| cellNearUePathlossThrPmCount | Range: 40... 159 Step size: 1 Unit: dB | O | This parameter sets the threshold for identifying cell-near UEs based on their downlink pathloss. Parameter is applicable for both FR1 and FR2 cells. Configured when 'actCellTptPerRadioLinkQualityCount' [CB012268-B-UPD001]or 'actUeCountPerRadioLinkQualityCount' [End CB012268-B-UPD001] is enabled. Configured by the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/NRPMCCP\_CELL/cellNearUePathlossThrPmCount. Default value: 100 The online modified value is taken into use for all UEs (existing and newly added) Note: a) Due to the functionality introduced in CB013033, any optional NIDD parameter with a default value shall be configured towards L2-PS using its default value. | CB012268-B |
